British Foreign Secretary Simon Visits Berlin 110

— German Correspondence

Negotiations Show No Effect; German-French Conflicts Are Still Difficult to Resolve

The Anglo-German negotiations, which have attracted worldwide attention, finally took place on March 24. British Foreign Secretary Simon, accompanied by Under-Secretary Eden, formally visited Berlin. This is the first time since the National Socialist Party came to power that they have been graced with the attention of a British gentleman. If it were two years ago, it would have been considered a strange tale for the British Foreign Secretary to pay a visit to Hitler with the honors due to a head of state and to conduct negotiations between the two countries. This situation is similar to that of Mussolini ten years ago and Stalin three years ago. The world has truly changed too quickly, forcing British politicians to change their traditional gentlemanly attitude. Why are Hitler's prices different morning and evening? Two years ago, not only was he seen as a buffoon, but more importantly, Germany did not have the backing of strength. Today, Hitler is still Hitler, but Germany's military preparations have caught up with France. We know that there is no "justice" or "reason" in the international arena. There is only "power," and "power" is better than everything.

According to the official British announcement, the mission of Simon and his party is to discuss the scope based on the London agreement of February 3, to unblock the opinions between Germany and France, and to consolidate peace in Europe. However, after the German government implemented conscription on March 16 and openly rearmed, the French attitude turned to complaining to Britain. Simon then stated that his visit to Berlin only contained the opinion of the German government as a preliminary step to resolving the entire European problem in the future, and that it was not a unilateral British action, and that there would be no tendency for Britain and Germany to directly conclude a treaty. This has temporarily eased France's threat -- the slogan "Otherwise, we (France) will go to Moscow".

French newspapers, before Simon's trip, said "Why bother with an empty trip." Simon himself also felt that he knew there was no hope, but for the sake of "peace", he had to go and see. It can be seen that the conditions put forward by both Germany and France are very harsh, and Simon does not have the power to make a certain aspect surrender. After two consecutive days of direct talks in Berlin, Simon returned to London according to the scheduled itinerary. The official announcements from both Britain and Germany believe that the negotiations were very effective. But what is the effect? According to Simon, he has an extremely pleasant impression of Hitler. On the other hand, he has a full understanding of Germany's demands. This is truly the tone of a first-class diplomat.

Many people feel that Germany has famous soldiers but no outstanding diplomats. This is correct. Hitler is full of the atmosphere of a warrior and has no diplomatic demeanor. This is also correct. However, Germany has one point that is the same as Japan and Soviet Russia. It not only knows how to use military force as a diplomatic backing but also understands how to take advantage of opportunities. For example, Hitler's words and Litvinov's words are in inverse proportion, but they can both cause headaches for the British because the speaker has an inviolable strength behind him. It is said that when Hitler and Simon talked about the issue of Austrian independence, Hitler said, "Why doesn't Britain come to sign this 'non-interference treaty' itself?" Such remarks naturally violate diplomatic conventions. Unfortunately, we do not know how Simon responded, otherwise, it would be more interesting to compare. In short, according to the news from the diplomatic community, Hitler's attitude towards various issues was very firm and straightforward, and he directly rebuked Simon. As a result of everyone's mutual verbal battle, both sides have their own reasons, so it is still the same as before the negotiations, and there is no possibility of convergence. What Simon said, he has an extremely pleasant impression of Hitler, if it refers to this, then, the attitude of a gentleman is not something that we ordinary people can guess.

The central issues of this negotiation are as follows: (1) Eastern European Pact. Britain's attitude is based on the London Agreement, linking various treaties, Eastern Europe, Danube, and Aviation, into three pacts. Germany advocates separation, especially for the Eastern European Pact, believing that there is no possibility of signing a treaty. Germany is unwilling to be bound by being connected with Soviet Russia in this treaty. The German newspapers have expressed this very firmly, recognizing that Germany has no problems on the western border, but the eastern part cannot be so careless and there must be a fair solution. (2) Danube Pact. Although Germany does not fundamentally oppose it, it proposes a condition, which is to add a practical definition to "non-interference". This means that Germany is not allowed to interfere in Austria, but other countries (referring to Italy) are also not allowed to interfere, and Britain must be a guarantor in this regard. (3) Aviation Pact. This was originally a treaty for Britain to mediate the conflict between Germany and France, and a concession to Germany. Germany naturally agrees, but Germany still has an attached condition, demanding equal rights for the air force. (4) Returning to the League of Nations. Germany believes that as long as Germany fully obtains equal rights in armaments, it can return to Geneva at any time. Britain, however, believes that it should return to Geneva first, and then everyone will discuss a solution in the League of Nations. (5) Abolishing conscription. Britain hopes that the German government will voluntarily abolish conscription first, and then everyone will jointly discuss a practical disarmament plan to limit the troop quotas of various countries. Germany believes that there is no room for compromise on this point. (6) Treaty issue. Britain advocates combining various treaties and not separating them individually, and the foundation of peace will be built on this. Germany advocates first concluding treaties individually and hopes that a Anglo-German treaty will be established immediately between Britain and Germany before extending to others. (7) Armaments issue. Britain advocates that Germany's armaments should be reduced to at least below France's current military strength. Conversely, Germany advocates that Germany's armaments must be equal to those of Soviet Russia.

Combining the above issues, we will see that both British and German celebrities are firmly guarding their positions and are unwilling to compromise in the slightest. A Swiss reporter put it well, "Are there any results from the Anglo-German negotiations?" Yes, if there were no negotiations, the important people of the two countries would have no opportunity to contact each other, have friendly relations, and talk freely. In addition, they would not be able to use their spare time to sit together at dinners. Is the friendship of important people not necessary? What else can we ask for?

In fact, most of these issues are still superficial. The so-called treaties, the League of Nations, disarmament, etc., are nothing more than diplomatic tricks. In the eyes of us laymen, everyone is making a lot of noise, so it is easy to be deceived by them, thinking that these gentlemen are really arguing for the sake of "treaties". Unfortunately, the fact is not the case. For example, the Eastern European Pact is a front set up by France and Russia, with the military strength of France and Russia as the backing. If Germany attacks one side, the two countries will "justifiably" send troops to attack from the front and back. For example, the Danube Pact is France's recognition of Italy's special status in Austria. If Germany's power invades Austria again, everyone will unite and use force to stop it. Germany is naturally unwilling to put itself in a ring drawn by others, giving others an excuse to send troops to attack itself. Therefore, everyone makes a big fuss about "treaties". As for their original intention, in other words, France wants to maintain the status quo, so it uses various methods to bind Germany. Germany wants to break the status quo, so it confronts France's policies step by step. The last way is naturally for everyone to use strength to solve the problem.

As a result of the Berlin negotiations, Britain obviously did not get any advantage. Not only is the contradiction between Germany and France impossible to resolve, but also the anti-Russian front, because of France's opposition -- French newspapers issued a warning during Simon's stay in Berlin. France firmly opposes any plans that directly or indirectly oppose Soviet Russia, and there does not seem to be much hope for Germany's excessive demands. So, from Britain's standpoint, it was truly an empty trip.

As for Germany's attitude, it is still pragmatic and taking steps step by step. Since Simon came to Berlin, the anti-Russian atmosphere in Germany has suddenly become more intense. All parties are very enthusiastically discussing Soviet Russia's military preparations, believing that eastern Germany is already a dangerous zone, and Soviet Russia's powerful Red Army is enough to threaten Germany's safety. For the sake of self-defense, Germany has the need to equalize its military preparations with Soviet Russia. This means that what Germany is demanding is not only 500,000 standing troops, being equal to France is considered satisfactory, but a further preparation to expand to one million. In terms of strength, it will be equal to Soviet Russia. This not only shocked France, but even experienced diplomats such as British Foreign Secretary Simon probably cannot help but frown.

Regarding the current situation in Europe, the anxious person is naturally not Germany. Germany has made full preparations in the past two years and is only waiting for the development of the situation. The "anti-Russian war" is probably not opposed by France, and Germany itself has to consider it. It is naturally difficult for a large army to penetrate deep into Soviet Russia without first resolving the Czech Republic and Poland. On the other hand, after all, the Czech Republic and Poland have a direct and personal interest in Germany, and they are also close neighbors. Why should Germany abandon what is near and seek what is far away? In addition, the cadres of the German National Defense Forces and the cadres of the Soviet Russian Red Army have always had close cooperation. General von Blomberg, the current Minister of National Defense of Germany, is said to have been given the position of Minister purely because he has a good relationship with the Soviet Russian Red Army. If we put aside the doctrine, then geographically, Germany will need the help of Soviet Russia in future wars. Moreover, it is said that German General Ludendorff had the news of being appointed as Chief of Staff during the European War, so there may be different opinions between anti-Russian and pro-Russian factions in the party and the military. The French saw this crisis, so Laval expressed that regardless of whether Germany joins or not, France has decided to conduct the Eastern European Treaty with Soviet Russia first. This is naturally equivalent to France and Russia concluding a military alliance. If this plan is really realized, then Germany will be in a situation of being attacked from both sides militarily, and development will not be easy. At present, the anti-Russian atmosphere in Germany may have other functions, otherwise, the many efforts spent by German military experts over the years will probably not have the opportunity to be realized, because France's powerful assistant is neither Britain nor Italy, but Soviet Russia. Soviet Russia can influence Germany and France in future wars. If the anti-Russian front really fails, then Soviet Russia's political status in Europe will become more important.

On April 11, diplomats from Britain, France, and Italy decided to meet in Stresa, northern Italy, to discuss the German issue. Based on past experience, we are told that this conference will not have much result. Britain, France, and Italy have different interests, so how can they unite?

In the meantime, what is worth noting is that Lithuania actually sentenced four leaders of the Memel National Socialist Party to death in the Memel lawsuit. This caused fierce opposition from Germany. In theory, Lithuania is a small country, how dare it "try to stop a chariot with a mantis arm" and anger Germany. Since his attitude dares to be so strong, then things are not necessarily very simple. In addition, the Little Entente and the Balkan Alliance are also preparing to hold a meeting in the Romanian capital. Their purpose is naturally to discuss a way to deal with Germany.

The war clouds in Europe are getting closer, and what we cannot know is only the time of the outbreak. (March 28 in Germany)

Kong Xiangxi's Report: The Closing of the Guantai Breach – and a Plan to Address Both Symptoms and Root Causes – 111

Nanjing Dispatch: Kong Xiangxi, Chairman of the National Economic Council's Water Conservancy Committee, reported to the Central Political Conference on the 17th regarding the closing of the Guantai breach in the Yellow River and a plan to address both symptoms and root causes. The original text is as follows:

"Regarding the report on the closure of the Guantai breach in the Yellow River and the difficult circumstances of the embankment construction, I, Xiangxi, previously made a temporary report at the 447th meeting on March 6th regarding the critical situation of the Yellow River breach at Changyuan, and requested discussion of relief measures. The meeting resolved that the National Economic Council and the Ministry of Finance should jointly discuss relief measures and raise the necessary funds. Funds were promptly allocated to expedite the work and complete the project. Recently, Kong Xiangrong, Standing Committee Member and Director of the Relief Work Group of the National Economic Council's Water Conservancy Committee, telegraphed that the Guantai breach had been closed at Chenshi (7-9 AM) on the 11th of this month. The difficult circumstances of the process are detailed below:

Previous Embankment Construction

Investigations revealed that the Yellow River breach, directly impacting the Changyuan Jiugu Road area, had four openings. These were all dry-season breaches that Director Zhou Xiangshi of the former Engineering and Accounting Group assigned to Sun Qingze, Director of the Second District Engineering Office, for embankment construction. After Director Zhou resigned due to illness, Director Kong Xiangrong took over. In addition to closing the Fenglou water opening, which had already diverted the entire main current, he also used the remaining funds allocated for the project to reinforce and heighten the embankment in the Shitouzhuan area at the request of the Hebei Provincial Government, with large vehicles transporting materials. After the completion of the work, including the previous projects, the Executive Yuan and the Yellow River Disaster Relief Committee, together with representatives from the Hebei Provincial Government, inspected and handed over the embankment section by section. The Hebei Provincial Government instructed its departments to take over the management, and reported the matter to the Executive Yuan for record. This was the process of the vigorous embankment construction after the breach the year before last.

Reasons for Subsequent Breaches

After the Yellow River Disaster Relief Committee's Relief Work Group completed the embankment project, preparations were made for its closure. The group telegraphed the Hebei Provincial Government requesting it to select appropriate personnel to station at the work site for defense, and advised them to urgently construct culverts and protective dikes along the embankment for defense. The Hebei Provincial Government replied that the Hebei River Affairs Bureau would be responsible for the subsequent defense. However, by mid-August, the river water rose again, and the Hebei River Affairs Bureau and the Post-Disaster Engineering Office failed to implement the important tasks mentioned in the telegram, resulting in four more breaches. Water seeped in through the base of the old embankment, but the water level was still about two meters below the top of the embankment and the main current of the river had not yet directly impacted it. At that time, only one deputy section chief of the River Affairs Bureau was present on the embankment with six river soldiers and thirty boatmen. Without any other laborers, it was a complete joke to try to protect this 20-li (approx. 6.2 miles) embankment with just over thirty people, causing the embankment that had been painstakingly built over the year to collapse again. A request was submitted to the Executive Yuan for strict investigation and punishment. These were the reasons for the subsequent breaches after the Changyuan opening was closed last year.

Situation Before Transfer to the Water Conservancy Committee

Subsequently, the Executive Yuan resolved to order the Hebei Provincial Government to dismiss and investigate Sun Qingze, the bureau chief, and instructed the Hebei River Affairs Bureau to undertake the embankment construction under the supervision of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission and the Yellow River Disaster Relief Committee, in accordance with the four relief measures proposed by the Yellow River Disaster Relief Committee's Relief Work Group. At that time, since the areas near the openings were all submerged, the blockage work started at Guantai. The Hebei River Affairs Bureau drafted a plan, which was reviewed and approved by the Yellow River Disaster Relief Committee's Relief Work Group and the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, and a deadline of one month was set for Hua Deming, the new director of the River Affairs Bureau, to complete the closure. This was the situation before the Relief Work Group was transferred to the jurisdiction of the National Economic Council's Water Conservancy Committee.

Perilous Situation of the Breach

After the group was transferred to the jurisdiction of the Water Conservancy Committee in February of this year, it was reported that as of December 18th of last year, only 64 meters of the 781-meter breach remained. At that time, the water was relatively calm and it was easier to block. However, Director Hua Deming of the River Affairs Bureau delayed the work under the pretext of purchasing and transporting materials, failing to gather them on time, and had to suspend the work to wait. Despite the Relief Work Group's best efforts to assist, transporting materials on his behalf, providing guidance on the blocking strategy, and urging him to expedite the work and complete the project on time, the more they urged, the more he ignored. As a result, he missed the three good opportunities to close the breach before the winter solstice in the old lunar calendar and before the new year in the old lunar calendar. Moreover, according to the successive reports from Ji Jianchuang of Hebei, the daily work reports of Director Hua only stated how many meters a certain dam had advanced and been raised, without any reports of breaches. Only after inspecting the work site did they learn that half of the reported work was just makeshift reinforcement and that the repeated breaches had not been truthfully reported. When Director Hua Deming's resignation was approved and Qi Shouan was appointed to replace him, the opening had already been scoured to a depth of 29 meters, diverting 80% of the river's flow, and the work situation became increasingly dangerous and the embankment construction became more difficult. This was the result of the negligence and delay of the Hebei provincial personnel in charge of river affairs.

The Closing of the Guantai Breach

Recognizing the perilous nature of the work and the difficulty of the embankment construction, and fearing that lack of unified authority would delay the important project, the committee, noting Director Kong Xiangrong's success in closing the Fenglou breach, reappointed him to take full responsibility for the Guantai remedial engineering project, following the Relief Work Group's method. An engineering office was established under the group, with Qi Chouan, Director of the Hebei River Affairs Bureau, as the director. A telegram was sent to urgently convene the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, the Directors of Construction of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces, and the Directors of River Affairs Bureaus to discuss remedial measures. It was decided to adopt the method of diverting the flow and using silt deposition to close the breach. At the same time, the Ministry of Finance was consulted to allocate funds to meet the urgent needs. Several Chinese and foreign experts were invited to conduct on-site inspections and study a plan to address both symptoms and root causes. After Director Kong took charge, he promptly deployed personnel, allocated tasks, transported willow and stone, and requisitioned boats and vehicles, working tirelessly from morning till night. On the material side, they were able to meet the needs of the project, and on the engineering side, they placed willow and stone mattresses on both the east and west dams, reinforcing them as breaches occurred, ensuring repeated safety. Willow dams were also built upstream and near the opening to divert the flow and promote silt deposition. Stone mattresses were laid inside the opening to protect the riverbed. When the two dams were adequately protected with stone mattresses, a date-kernel dam blocking method was implemented to close the breach. On the 11th of this month, it was reported that the Guantai breach was successfully closed at Chenshi (7-9 AM). It took Director Kong Xiangrong only twenty-odd days to take full responsibility for the Guantai project, working tirelessly and courageously to close the 29-meter deep water opening. This was to comfort the government's concern for the people's suffering and reflects the committee's best efforts at remediation and the successful closure.

A Plan to Address Both Symptoms and Root Causes

Based on the reports from the Chinese and foreign experts sent by the committee to inspect the work site, and after detailed study of the reports from various parties, it was generally believed that it was difficult to predict whether the project could be successfully closed. This is because the Yellow River's water flow is different from that of ordinary rivers. The problem is not only the excessive flow, but also the excessive sediment content, which causes deposition everywhere, resulting in constant shifts. The riverbed in the lower reaches has been rising over the years, making it difficult to discharge water smoothly, leading to more frequent breaches and making embankment construction more difficult. If reservoirs could be built in the mountain valleys upstream to store water, and new channels could be opened in the lowlands downstream, while reinforcing the Jin堤 (Jin Dike) and the dikes of the three provinces along the river for protection, the flood disaster might be slightly reduced. Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission member Li Yizhi was instructed to expedite the reinforcement of the Jin堤 before the flood season. Considering that the dikes of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces had been neglected and unrepaired for years, telegrams were sent to the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission and the provincial governments of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, urging them to make early plans to repair and protect the dikes of the three provinces, discuss and implement them properly, and invite Chinese and foreign experts to conduct thorough research, so that the Yellow River disaster, which has historically been a major problem, could be reduced, and the tens of millions of acres of farmland along the river could be protected. This is the plan to address both the symptoms and root causes of the Yellow River flood disaster.

Total Cost of 450,000

Recently, a telegram was received from the supervisory committee members dispatched by President Yu of the Control Yuan, stating that the Guantai closure was progressing well and that continued efforts were needed to heighten and reinforce the embankment to achieve complete success. The swiftness of this closure was due to sufficient funding and unified authority, which enabled it to achieve twice the result with half the effort. Regarding the project funding, since Director Kong Xiangrong took over the remedial project, I, Xiangxi, allocated a total of 450,000 yuan. After the completion of the project, the director will be responsible for submitting the expense report to account for the public funds. All matters relating to the closure of the Yellow River Guantai breach and the various difficult circumstances are hereby reported for your consideration. (Central News Agency)

The Chinese Art Association and Modern Chinese Art – A Speech by Zhang Daofan – 112

Beijing Dispatch: Zhang Daofan, Chairman of the Chinese Art Association, gave a radio speech on the Central Broadcasting Station on the evening of the 14th, titled "The Chinese Art Association and Modern Chinese Art." The original text is as follows:

"Many people know about the establishment of the Chinese Art Association in the capital, but I am afraid that many compatriots in more remote areas do not. Now, using this brief time, I will give everyone a simple report.

The Chinese Art Association was initiated by dozens of artists from Nanjing, Shanghai, Beiping, and other places on the day of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's birthday in 1933 and officially established in Nanjing. It has now been in existence for a year and a half. After its establishment, artists from various places enthusiastically joined the association, and it now has more than 200 members. On September 15, 1934, a founding anniversary exhibition was held in Nanjing, with many works submitted by artists from various places. It has been decided to hold spring and autumn exhibitions within this year. The spring exhibition is scheduled to open with a preview today (the 14th) and officially open tomorrow (the 15th). Now, I will briefly report on the preparation situation. The call for works for this exhibition was posted in February. The original deadline for submissions was the 5th of this month. Later, because the works sent by the post office from various provinces could not arrive on time due to the long distances, the deadline was extended to the 11th of this month. As a result, all the arrangement procedures were rushed to completion on the 12th and 13th, so it was extremely busy. Although there has been progress in the arrangement aspect compared to previous exhibitions, the colleagues of this association still feel that it is not satisfactory. I hope that all sectors will forgive us.

In total, more than 1,000 works of calligraphy, Chinese painting, oil painting, metalwork, sculpture, etc., were received. In terms of the location of submission, there were seventeen or eighteen provinces and cities including Henan, Shanghai, Beiping, Tianjin, Guangzhou, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Guangdong, Hebei, Jiangxi, Yunnan, Sichuan, Shaanxi, Shanxi, and Guizhou. In terms of the artists, there were more than two hundred people including Chen Shuren, Gao Jianfu, Xu Beihong, Wang Qi, Ru Yuli, Li Yigong, Zhu Wenyun, Chen Zhifo, Hong Ludong, Zhang Shuqi, Liu Xiaoseng, Wang Dong, Zhang Xiaolou, Xie Gongzhan, Zhao Shaoang, Wang Yachen, Zhang Guang, Yu Jifan, Xu Shiqi, Pan Yuliang, Gao Leyi, Long Wen, Gao Xishun, Zhang Yiran, Li Jinfa, Zhou Bomin, Pan Tianshou, Sun Fuxi, Chen Liaoqing, Pan Boshan, Guan Yide, Yang Shoutao, Liu Zigu, Huang Shaoqiang, Huang Shaoshou, Jiang Danqing, Zhou Zhensun, Yang Manhua, Xiao Qianzhong, Tian Huan, Wu Fuzhi, Zhu Qizhan, Lu Shihou, Liang Dingming, Yang Jihong, Zhang Yu, Wang Chengzai, Wang Chengzhai, Teng Baibei, Huang Hongtu, Jiang Zhaohe, and Wang Linyi. This enthusiastic participation of artists from various places is really a good phenomenon. However, what this association regrets the most is that the venue of the Bamboo Capital Overseas Chinese Reception Center is too small to display all the works. Therefore, as a result of the selection, only about 360 pieces can be displayed. I cannot bear to part with the rest of the works. Regarding this matter, I would like to make a solemn statement now, which is that the works that cannot be displayed cannot be said to be all unqualified or unsuccessful. The limited venue size is one reason. Late arrival of submissions is another reason. Oversized, too long, or too small submissions that are inconvenient to hang or display are another reason. Lack of frames or improper mounting is another reason. Everyone knows this situation, and both the submitters and the audience will probably forgive this association.

Everyone knows that the development of art is closely related to the culture of a country. In the past hundred years or so, Chinese art seems to have been declining day by day. Its important position in world culture has almost been shaken. This gives a major warning to us who are now paying attention to culture, loving art, and working hard in art. The reason for this is nothing more than the fact that in the past, artists generally lacked a good organization to cooperate with, and the government or society failed to fully promote or support it. The establishment of this association is to make up for the lack of organization in the past. The enthusiastic participation of artists from various places after the establishment of this association proves that cooperation is not impossible. In terms of the central and local governments, in addition to having decided to build a Central Museum in Nanjing, it has also recently decided to build an art exhibition hall in the capital. This is proof of the country's emphasis on promoting and supporting art. In terms of society, there has also been a lot of enthusiasm for promotion and support in recent years.

All of this is very gratifying for the future of Chinese art. What this association most sincerely hopes for now is: (1) That artists all over the country work together with sincerity and cooperation; (2) That the central or local governments promote and support art as much as possible; (3) That social figures and art lovers pay special attention to and support art, so that the works of Chinese artists will have considerable outlets in the future, maintain a minimum standard of living, and increase the courage of all artists to work hard, so that Chinese art can achieve great achievements in the 20th century and stabilize the important position of Chinese art in world culture. The colleagues of this association are willing to dedicate their loyalty and do their utmost to cooperate sincerely and move forward with the artists of the whole country under the promotion of the central government and the support of social figures."

Songjiang: Resignation of the First District Chief 113

Li Zufu, the chief of the first district of this county, recently petitioned the county government again, requesting to resign due to the concurrent handling of baojia (household registration system) and river dredging, and the recurrence of an old illness, making it difficult to manage both. The county government instructed in a document stating, "The report is noted. It is claimed that the old illness has recurred and it is difficult to manage both baojia and river dredging. The resignation is approved. Awaiting selection of a replacement. Before the selection and appointment, Assistant Lu Jingzi of the district will temporarily act as the district chief. In addition to separate orders, you must immediately comply." Suzhou: Request for the Return of Grain Borrowed from Wuxian Over the Years 114

Over the years, the provincial government has borrowed grain in the amount of 80,000 yuan from landowners in Wuxian for the land tax (calculated at 4.5 yuan per stone, approximately 0.45 yuan per mu). Although the landowners have repeatedly petitioned the provincial government to request its return, and the provincial government has considered repaying it in five years, it has not been repaid due to the tight provincial treasury. Recently, the Suzhou Finance Bureau has been rigorously pursuing outstanding taxes. Therefore, the landowners have requested the provincial government to offset the outstanding taxes with the borrowed grain. Because the procedures were not in order, the provincial government instructed them to supplement the procedures and then conduct a further review. Recently, local gentry Peng Zijia and others submitted a petition to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance yesterday (the 18th), fully explaining the situation of the borrowed grain and requesting that the Jiangsu Provincial Government be ordered to return the borrowed grain in full to alleviate the suffering of the people of Suzhou.

Wuxi: Lack of Spring Silkworm Eggs Leads to Private Price Gouging 115

This year's spring silkworm eggs, as stipulated by the Provincial Sericulture Improvement and Management Committee, are allowed to be freely traded by various farms, with a uniform selling price of 4 jiao (1 jiao is 1/10 of a yuan) per sheet of eggs. No underpricing or price gouging is allowed, otherwise, severe punishment will be imposed. However, since the start of sales, many eggs have been shipped to neighboring counties in other provinces, resulting in a situation where the supply of spring silkworm eggs in this county cannot meet the demand. In recent days, farmers in the rural areas have been very enthusiastic about buying eggs. Therefore, those who seek profit have privately raised prices, selling five sheets for 5 jiao, 5 jiao and 5 fen, or even 7 or 8 jiao. The Sericulture Model Zone has reported the above situation, and in addition to ordering immediate reporting for strict investigation and handling according to the law, it has also dispatched personnel to the rural areas to investigate and gather evidence.

Minister Kong Arrives in Shanghai and Discusses: No Need to Panic About Silver Issues; No Need to Increase Balancing Tax Currently; Relief for Yellow River Disaster Area Under Investigation 117

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, who recently went to Nanjing to attend meetings of the Executive Yuan and the Central Political Council, left Nanjing by overnight train at 11:00 PM the night before and arrived at Zhenru Station at 7:10 AM yesterday morning. He went directly to his private residence on Seymour Road for rest. Later, around 11:00 AM, he met with reporters and made remarks on the silver issue. At noon, he went to the Central Bank to handle important official matters. The following is a record of Minister Kong's remarks:

Balancing Tax Rate: No Increase for Now 118

According to Minister Kong, there is currently no need to increase the silver export balancing tax. Since the United States raised the price of silver, the detriment to us has been the sharp outflow of silver. Currently, foreign banks in Shanghai have shown good intentions and are voluntarily no longer exporting silver. There is no need to panic about the silver issue. The government's levying of a silver export balancing tax is also aimed at stopping the export of silver. Now that foreign banks are voluntarily no longer exporting silver, there is no need to increase the balancing tax for the time being.

Bandit Suppression Proceeds Smoothly; Guantai Confluence Completed 119

The military operations to suppress bandits in Sichuan and Guizhou provinces have been progressing smoothly recently. The temporary expenditures for bandit suppression are also quite limited. The confluence of the Yellow River's Guantai breach has been completed. The staff has worked hard. The issue of relief for the disaster area of the Yellow River breach is currently under investigation.

Hou Houpei Returns Home After Investigating Cooperation Affairs in Japan 121

In order to understand the actual situation of cooperative undertakings in various countries, the China Cooperative Society dispatched Hou Houpei, Deputy Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank, and others to Japan for investigation at the end of last month. After half a month, the mission has been completed. He arrived in Shanghai on the Japanese ship Shanghai Maru at 3:00 PM yesterday. After disembarking, he returned to the bank for rest. Hou plans to take a short rest in Shanghai, compile a report, and then go to Nanjing to report back.

Two Important Meetings of the Bank of Communications: Discussion of Increasing Capital Stock; Standing Committee Meeting of the Board of Directors Today; General Meeting of Shareholders Tomorrow 130

According to the Central News Agency, the Ministry of Finance has long instructed the Bank of Communications to increase official shares by 10 million yuan and revised the original regulations. After receiving the order, the bank has scheduled to convene a standing committee meeting of the board of directors and a general meeting of shareholders today and tomorrow to discuss. The details are as follows:

Revised Regulations 131

The original capital stock of the Bank of Communications was 10 million yuan, of which 2 million yuan was official shares and the rest was commercial shares. The Ministry of Finance believes that the social finance has been exhausted in recent years and the market turnover is difficult, and banks urgently need to invest huge amounts to adjust. However, the bank's funds are limited and it is feared that it will be difficult to cope with the situation. Therefore, it has been decided to invest 10 million yuan in official shares, which will be allocated from the 24th year of the Republic of China's financial bonds. An order has been received and the principles of the regulations have been revised.

Standing Committee Meeting of the Board of Directors 132

After receiving the order, the bank has scheduled to convene a standing committee meeting of the board of directors at 2:00 PM today in the bank's conference room to discuss seven matters. It is heard that the revised regulations are the same as those of the Bank of China. The original fixed interest rate for both official and commercial shares was 7%, but now, in order to give preferential treatment to commercial shares, the annual interest rate for other shares has been reduced to 5%. The directors to be added after the increase in official shares will be announced today and tomorrow.

General Meeting of Shareholders 133

The general meeting of shareholders is scheduled to be held tomorrow (the 20th) in the afternoon. The board of directors will report the Ministry's order to increase capital stock and submit the revised regulations for discussion. Since the term of office of the original directors of the bank has not yet expired, there will be no changes except for the directors appointed by the Ministry. However, the supervisors have completed their term of office, so they will be re-elected.

Art Exhibition: Preview Day 11 142

Yesterday (the 18th) was the eleventh day of the Shanghai preview of the International Exhibition of Chinese Art in London. People from all walks of life continued to visit the exhibition enthusiastically. The various news items are summarized as follows:

The Venue Emphasizes Hygiene 143

In view of the large number of visitors in recent days, the exhibition recognized that the air in the venue is prone to becoming polluted. It has taken measures to open the air vents in each room for a short time every night to allow air circulation and to clean the floors and toilets. The toilets are also disinfected with disinfectant, and the flowers and plants displayed in the corners of other rooms are also replaced every few days.

Continued Printing of English Catalog 144

Thirty-nine more exhibits have arrived, and the Chinese catalog has been printed and included in the exhibit catalog. The English part has also been printed by the Shanghai Commercial Press, and has been included in the previously printed English catalog.

Adding Western Years to the Cards 145

The cards used to display the exhibits are in both Chinese and English. Chinese eras such as Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing are also translated into English. For the convenience of Western viewers, the exhibition has added Western calendar years to the cards. The English catalog and the list of English exhibits already have Western calendar years, and now the addition of Western calendar years to the cards will make it even more convenient for Western viewers.

Hobson's Talk 146

Mr. R.T. Hobson, the British Commissioner, gave a talk on Chinese art at a tea party of the Shanghai Rotary Club, which was divided into four sections. The first section described the glorious history of Chinese art, praising the early development of Chinese art and the exquisiteness of calligraphy and painting. The second section described the differences between Chinese and European art, saying that Chinese painting deeply captures the interest of nature and is different from European painting, which focuses on artificiality. It also said that the invention of Chinese porcelain was 1,000 years earlier than that of Europe and was an important invention. The third section described the importance of the exhibition, briefly stating that the London exhibition has great significance internationally, which can make Chinese and European cultures communicate and make Europe more fully understand China. The fourth section described that the exhibits are sufficient to represent Chinese art, and are very different from the antiques previously sold by antique dealers into Europe, which only dazzled Europeans with novelty. Therefore, this exhibition is sufficient to enable Chinese art to express its great significance.

Three British Commissioners Went North Yesterday 147

Of the five British commissioners sent to China to select antiques, Mr. Rafael has already gone to Japan, while Mr. David, Mr. Hobson, and Mr. Omorfopoulos traveled north to visit Peiping and Tianjin yesterday. Mr. Bo Xihuo remained in Shanghai to take care of the transport of antiques to England. Yesterday, Mr. Dai and others went to the exhibition to say goodbye to the authorities. Yang Zhensheng received and sent them off, and Minister of Education Wang Shijie also gave them a copy of Chinese scenery as a souvenir.

Date of Transportation to England Determined 148

Regarding the issue of transporting antiques to England, preparations are now actively underway. The British commissioners have made further consultations with Yang Zhensheng, the Director-General of the exhibition. It is reported that the date has been set for May 28.

Chamber of Commerce Calls on the Legislative Yuan: To Pass the Commercial Registration Law Quickly; To Remedy Article 681 of the Civil Code 150

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce telegraphed the Legislative Yuan yesterday, saying, "We have just approved the Han口 Chamber of Commerce's telegraph stating that the provisions of Article 681 of the Debt Section of the Civil Code, which stipulates that partners are jointly and severally liable for partnership debts, are difficult to implement. We request that the Commercial Registration Law be revised to remedy this situation. The drafting has been jointly carried out by the Civil Code and Commercial Law Committees. Article 9 of the draft stipulates that the names, addresses, and types and amounts of investment of the partners, if they have been registered with the competent authority in the place of business by each person, shall be liable for sharing losses within the limits of their investment. The same applies when shares are transferred or changed. This provision is most in line with the requirements of businessmen. At the meeting and review on October 31 of last year, there were still strong objections, resulting in no decision being made. The Chamber believes that this case is of great importance to the future of commerce and has passed the original text of Article 9 of the draft law on November 15 of the same year to remedy the situation. It has been approved for reference by the Civil Code and Commercial Law Committees. Several months have passed without hearing any further discussion. If this is shelved for a long time, the disputes caused by Article 681 of the Civil Code to businessmen will not be resolved. At a time when commerce is declining and finance is bankrupt, the number of partnership stores is bound to decrease day by day, and the organization of the old commercial arena is really at risk of shaking its foundations. The Chamber represents all the merchants in Shanghai and regards this as a matter of vital interest. We are therefore telegraphing your hospital for verification. We implore you to convene a meeting for discussion as soon as possible and pass the original proposal to facilitate commercial transportation. We pray for this. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, bows respectfully."

Reply From the Ministry of Judicial Administration: Whether the Bond Provides a Guarantee Should Still Be Decided by the Court 151

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a letter from the Timber Industry Association, requesting that the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Justice be forwarded to notify all courts that when litigants provide public bonds as collateral, they should not refuse them. The Chamber has now received a reply from the Ministry of Judicial Administration, stating: "The presentation has been acknowledged. Public bonds are one of the valuable securities. According to the provisions of Article 75, Paragraph 2 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, they should be allowed to be substituted for bail. However, they must be converted at the market price. This was instructed by the Judicial Yuan's Yuanzi No. 430 on February 5, 20th year to the Zhejiang High Court on record. The nature of treasury bills is the same as that of public bonds, and civil security deposits are similar to criminal bail. If litigants provide public bonds and treasury bills as civil security or pay criminal bail, and they are converted at the market price, the courts will naturally find it difficult not to accept them. However, Section 2 of Article 102 of the Code of Civil Procedure states that those who provide security shall deposit cash or valuable securities deemed appropriate by the court. Also, Section 2 of Article 75 of the Code of Criminal Procedure states that bail may be substituted with valuable securities depending on the circumstances. Therefore, whether or not to allow it should still be decided by the court. The above-mentioned sections have been ordered to the Jiangsu High Court and the two High Courts, Second and Third Divisions, to submit their opinions and report them, and the Ministry of Finance has also been approved to send a letter to the Ministry to discuss the situation. In addition to having copied all the related documents and ordered the courts of all provinces to refer to them and handle them, this approval is hereby notified."

Citywide Students Vow to Use National Products in Downtown Yesterday; Over Ten Thousand People at the Scene Resolve to Use National Products; Airplanes Scatter Leaflets; All Newspapers Publish Special Editions 152

Order: (1) Play music, (2) Presidium takes their seats, (3) Everyone stands at attention, (4) Sing the Party song, (5) Pay the highest respect to the National Party flag and the portrait of the Premier, (6) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's last will, (7) Silence, (8) Chairman's report, (9) Chairman reads the oath, everyone recites aloud in unison, (10) Representatives of party and government agencies deliver speeches, (11) Representatives of various organizations deliver speeches, (12) Student representatives deliver speeches, (13) Sing the Student National Products Year song, (14) Play music, (15) End of the ceremony.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony was performed as required, the chairman of the presidium, Pan Gongzhan, gave a report, saying, "Dear students, today is the day when the Student National Products Year Promotion Joint Association convenes representatives from large, medium, and small schools across the city to hold the "Use National Products" oath ceremony at the City Hall. This year, representatives from all walks of life in Shanghai have designated this year as the Student National Products Year because they feel that the national economic situation is declining year by year, with a staggering annual trade deficit of 700 million yuan. On average, every citizen buys two yuan worth of foreign goods. If we do not wake up again, we will perish without waiting for the military and political aggression of the great powers. Therefore, all parties have taken the initiative to promote national products, hoping that factories will improve their products, businesses will sell fewer foreign goods, and students, as outstanding members of society, with pure knowledge, will engage in promoting national products, so that people will have some understanding of national products. However, the Student National Products Year is not only for students to use national products, but also for non-students to bear the same responsibility. Students themselves should start with themselves in persuading people. In the early stages of our work, in order to achieve twice the result with half the effort, we are holding this solemn and grand "Use National Products" oath ceremony here to give students a deep impression and encourage themselves. At the same time, we hope that after participating in the oath, students will earnestly persuade their families, schools, and society according to the oath."

Tong Xingbai's Speech

Then, Tong Xingbai gave a speech, saying, "Representatives from all walks of life, dear students, we have heard the call to promote national products for a long time. However, the result is still nothing more than a five-minute burst of enthusiasm, forgotten after the expiration date, and all previous efforts are abandoned, which is a pity. The Student National Products Year, seeing the indifference of the people of the country to the psychology of national products, has specially convened students to hold an oath ceremony here. Representatives from all over the city enthusiastically participate, and the future hope for promoting national products is limitless. The purpose of the oath is to remedy the shortcomings of the five-minute enthusiasm. It cannot be taken lightly. It is closely related to personal character and integrity. If you still use foreign goods after taking the oath, although no one is watching, our character has been severely damaged. We have sworn publicly and violated the oath, which means we have no integrity. From now on, we should earnestly publicize and promote to families, relatives, friends, and society, and take the initiative to use national products in order to achieve the purpose of the oath. Our country is now in a state of economic panic, industrial depression, and worker unemployment, which has reached an extreme state of decline. The reason is that foreign goods are dumping, so that workers cannot survive, indirectly creating social unrest. If you want to remedy the current crisis, you can only seek development from the economy. The people of the country should happily use national products, so that domestic industries can prosper, and then the country can be restored. On the contrary, if foreign goods are rampant, how can workers live? Today's student oath is of great importance to the future of the country. Saving the country and saving the people is all in this one action. May you all practice it in person to achieve the goal, so that the country and society can be restored."

Citywide students take the "Use National Products" oath ceremony at the City Hall (Photo by Qichang)

Is this the performance that should be had in the National Products Year? But this year, all sectors have publicly designated this year as the Student National Products Year. Please don't be discouraged and continue to work hard to promote it. Especially in the field of education, it is the vanguard of the nation. The school authorities use national products, and then the teachers and students promote them to the family, and then further promote them to all aspects. Now the country, in addition to expanding military preparations with political force, the most important thing is the economy. Therefore, all countries, in addition to expanding military preparations, pay great attention to the economy. The United States is raising the price of silver and inflating the currency to export goods as much as possible, which is also a matter of paying attention to economic problems. China is the number one consumer market in the eyes of all countries, but if you want to avoid this kind of economic aggression, you can only save yourself. The way to save yourself is to unite the whole country to promote national products. The rejuvenation of China is just around the corner. I hope everyone who takes the oath will keep it in mind and don't throw it out of the blue after it's over. This is the original intention of the speech. I hope you will all encourage each other." In addition, Zhang Shouyong, Lu Xingzhuang, and others also gave speeches, and the length of the speeches is omitted.

Student's Reply

After the representatives finished their speeches, Jiang Nianqu of Datong University gave a reply, saying, "Today I am here to participate in the oath ceremony of the Student National Products Year Promotion Joint Association, and after hearing the instructions from all the gentlemen, I can't help but have many thoughts. Recalling the past, we cannot separate ourselves from foreign goods in our lives, from morning to night, resulting in a staggering annual trade deficit and being subjected to economic aggression by the great powers, causing the national vitality to decline day by day. If we do not immediately rise up and save ourselves, what can we imagine for the future of the country? Today, the Student National Products Year is holding an oath here. All of us students should actively promote national products from today onwards, so that the family and society will be completely nationalized. If this can be done, the country will have hope." Then, Yin Baotai of Jiaotong University gave a speech, saying, "In the past few years, the result of promoting national products is that the annual trade deficit has gradually increased. This cannot but be attributed to the ineffectiveness of the promoters and the lack of self-love of the general public. It must be known that promoting national products is not only about holding meetings, shouting slogans, and posting slogans. The promoters must first set an example, practice it in person, and promote it earnestly without avoiding slander. It is important to know that people slander me, and their intention is to encourage us to continue to work hard, not to destroy us. However, failure is the mother of success. We should follow the Premier's revolutionary spirit, continue our efforts, and never give up. I firmly believe that it will be effective. Today, we take an oath here, and we should work hard according to the words of the oath. It must be known that promoting national products is the only way to save the country and save the people." Then, Yang Lizhen of Minli Women's Middle School replied, saying, "Today is the student oath ceremony. All students should devote themselves to the promotion of national products from today onwards, so as not to betray the original intention of the oath." Finally, Chen Yaru, a representative of Tiehua Elementary School, gave a speech, saying, "Since our country has been in contact with the great powers, the number of imported goods has been increasing year by year. The reason is that the people of the country like novelty and love modernity, which has led to the decline of national power day by day. If this continues, the country will be destroyed. This year is the Student National Products Year, and students should take action to achieve practical results, earnestly promote it, and complete their mission. National economy and people's livelihood rely on it."

Visit the Exhibition

After the ceremony, the students lined up according to the flag number and entered the City Hall auditorium to visit the National Products Student Supplies Exhibition. The layout of the venue was magnificent, and all the exhibits were set up in the air without using nails, so the students of each school could have a deep impression of the exhibits. After the visit, they came out one by one, so there was no phenomenon of rushing to get the gifts at the exit, which was enough to show the spirit of the new life.

Grand Event at the Venue

The Student National Products Use Oath Ceremony held by the association was attended by more than 10,000 students from more than 600 schools. According to the person in charge of the association, all parties cooperated very well in this gathering. For example, the Zhabei Bus Company had a joint reception office at the North Station and Tiantong'an Station, which provided low prices and order, and helped the teachers and students attending the meeting a lot. The Public Works Bureau and the Asia American Company installed loudspeakers, so it was clear even dozens of feet away, so there was no need to worry about the crowd. The Public Security Bureau, the Public Works Bureau, the Municipal Government Boy Scout Council, etc. gave a lot of help. The full band of the Public Security Bureau trained the students to sing the National Products Year song in advance and played at the meeting, which was especially commendable.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests the Ministry of Industry to Enforce Membership Regulations for Fellow Traders; Since Fellow Traders Have No Freedom to Withdraw or Not Join, This Interpretation Should Be Included in the Implementation Rules 153

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry, stating: "Regarding the request for confirmation, on October 6 of last year, your ministry issued instruction No. 29209 regarding the association's request to confirm the sanctions for fellow traders who do not join the guild. The instruction stated: 'Both requests are noted. Regarding the case of fellow traders not joining the guild, we have recently received a letter from the Central People's Movement Committee and a consultation from the Hubei Provincial Government, forwarded by the Hankou Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting a clear definition of measures to compel fellow traders to join the guild uniformly and to hold non-member businesses jointly responsible for all obligations of members. According to the legal intent of Articles 3, Section 2, 4, Section 1, and 7 of the Industrial and Commercial Guild Law, the members of the trade guild are the local companies and firms in the entire industry. All those who belong to the same industry should naturally join the guild, should fulfill the obligations of members, and should abide by the rules of the guild. Moreover, except for suspension of business, relocation, or expulsion, there is no freedom to withdraw or not join. The term "join the guild" in Article 4, Item 5, refers to the regulations for joining procedures. If a business is negligent in fulfilling these joining procedures, it still cannot be exempted from its obligations. The section of the association's proposal that non-member businesses should be held jointly responsible for all obligations of members is in accordance with the regulations. As for the main obligation of members, which is paying membership fees, for those who do not fulfill this obligation, the Interpretation No. 914 of the Judicial Yuan from May of last year can be used to file a lawsuit for payment according to law.' The above situation was submitted and instructed to be informed on file. According to the previous submission, it is urgent to instruct and inform on file." The association fully admires the ministry's intention to remedy the situation in a timely manner and weigh the situation fairly. The association has repeatedly engaged experts and committees to discuss the implementation plan, who all believe that the above instruction from the ministry is an elaboration on the legal intent of the Industrial and Commercial Guild Law, aiming to facilitate implementation and originally containing the nature of implementation rules. The above instruction, rather than being filed away, should be made into a provision, which is easier for the guild to comply with and easier for the court to adopt. It is proposed to add a new article after Article 9 of the current Implementation Rules of the Industrial and Commercial Guild Law, stating: 'Local companies and firms, except those who should be expelled according to the guild's rules and those who are rejected for membership, are all members of the trade guild, but must fulfill the joining procedures. Those who do not fulfill the joining procedures established by the guild shall fulfill the obligations of members and shall not be exempted under any pretext, and the guild may sue the government to urge them to fulfill the obligations, and may also suspend their rights and give them appropriate sanctions according to the rules.' With this provision, those who have not fulfilled the joining procedures and owe membership fees and violate industry regulations can be reported to the government with a basis for acceptance. This is what is proposed for your ministry to adopt and implement." "In addition, according to the above instruction from your ministry, all businesses that are negligent in fulfilling joining procedures and negligent in fulfilling membership obligations are in violation of the guild's rules. In addition to expulsion, the guild should specify other methods of punishment in the guild's rules. Therefore, in the future, to sanction members who violate these guild rules, each trade guild should urgently supplement specific articles in the current rules for compliance. It is proposed that after approval from your ministry, the municipal guilds will be notified to supplement two articles in the current rules: 'One is that all companies, firms, and stores in the city's area that are in the same industry, except those expelled by the guild's rules and those rejected for membership, are members of the guild, should abide by the guild's rules and industry regulations approved by the competent government, and should obey the guild's discipline and fulfill the guild's resolutions, but can only enjoy the rights of members after completing the following joining procedures.' The joining procedures are listed on the left: 'A. Introduction by two or more members of the guild, approved by a majority of the executive committee. B. Filling out a membership application form. C. Paying the membership fee.' 'The second is that all members who have the obligation to comply with the provisions of the guild's rules shall have the method of punishment decided by the executive committee according to the circumstances, as follows: 1. Warning. 2. Suspension of the rights granted by the guild's laws and regulations and other protections that the guild should have for the industry. 3. Reputational sanctions. 4. Monetary sanctions. 5. Expulsion. 6. All members break off relations with them.' The amount of item 4 above shall be decided by the executive committee and submitted to the competent government for approval and execution. Since this matter concerns a common case and is based on instruction No. 29209 from your ministry, we should request that the principles be approved first, so that each industry can draft articles accordingly, which will be more serious. At that time, it should be passed by the general assembly of each guild and submitted to the competent government for approval and implementation to comply with the procedures." "The above two requests are all elaborations and references to the instructions of your ministry, seeking to make the provisions more detailed. Experts have no objection, and it is also convenient for the business situation. We should prepare a document and submit it to your ministry for review and approval and implementation, which is convenient for the public. Respectfully submitted."

The First Special Court Prepares to Build a New Prison; Land Has Been Purchased on Qipei Road; A Committee Has Been Formed to Oversee Construction 155

The Women's Prison in the First Special District was originally reorganized from the Women's Detention Center in the era of the Mixed Court. The prison site is located in a corner of the First Special District Local Court of Gao Erfen. Although the prison is five stories high, the number of female criminals has been increasing in recent years. The female prisoners in the prison are full and cannot be accommodated. The local authorities have long planned to build a large new prison. In the past, they asked the local authorities to purchase land in the west of Shanghai to prepare for construction. However, due to some kind of problem, the plan could not be realized. They then rented several folk houses near Yuqing Lane on Shangpu Road as temporary prisons, specializing in imprisoning female criminals serving short sentences and detention, such as prostitutes and opium smokers, who were all transferred to them. The original prison was relieved of the burden of overcrowding. However, this is not a long-term solution. Therefore, the authorities of the two courts still believe that the construction of a prison is a matter that cannot be delayed. Last month, they surveyed a piece of land located on Qipei Road, opposite the Gao Erfen Court, which is very suitable for building a prison. They negotiated with the owner, Yi Shang, and it is said that they have already purchased it. The authorities of the two courts then appointed senior personnel with architectural knowledge and organized the "Special District New Prison Construction Committee Office" yesterday in the downstairs room of the Gao Erfen Court to be responsible for preparing for the construction of the prison. The staff of the association were very busy at the beginning of its establishment.

The Case of Red Breeze Drugged with Keerfang Elixir Continues; The Family Has Concluded the Interrogation and Set a Date for Sentencing 156

The case of Wang Yuxian, known as Red Breeze and Old Nine, being drugged with Keerfang elixir and robbed of a gold bracelet and jade ring worth sixty yuan in room 523 of the Yangzi Hotel at 289 Yunnan Road was investigated by Chinese detective Yang Peisheng and detective eye Ruan Taibin of the Yulin Road Police Station, who arrested four suspects, the young men Ruan Zilin, Lu Jianying, Li Jianguang, and doctor Liu Jiaji, and sent them to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the police sent Ruan and others to the third criminal court. Lawyer Li Zhishan of the Engineering Bureau explained the process and said that when Ruan Zilin was arrested, he had two pawn tickets and a pistol hidden in a water tank at 280 Beijing Road. The detectives went and took them out, but there were no bullets. It was said that they belonged to a friend surnamed Xu. The pawn tickets were also his. The surname Xu was arrested by the local court for a robbery case and is currently being interrogated. Detectives have been sent to inquire and said that it has nothing to do with the crime committed by Ruan. It has now been found out that Doctor Liu Jiaji was actually framed by Ruan. The Keerfang elixir was borrowed from Guo Jingqing in Jiangwan. Now Guo has come to court to testify, so Doctor Liu should be declared innocent. The other three defendants are charged with robbery by three or more people in accordance with Article 348 of the Criminal Law and drug anesthesia crimes in accordance with Article 346. Please investigate. According to Guo Jingqing's statement, he lives at 11 Songjia Port, Jiangwan. He used to be a nurse and doctor in a hospital, but now he has resigned and practices medicine at home. The Keerfang elixir was because Ruan had neck problems, and I treated him. He knew the nature of the elixir. On the 6th of this month, he went to Xin Xin Hotel to open a room and borrowed the elixir. I thought it was too dangerous, so I asked for it back. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 8th, while I was out, he went home with two friends, Lu and Li, and secretly took a bottle of the elixir to do this illegal thing. I did not hear about it in advance. Questioning Ruan Zilin, he confessed that the Xin Xin Hotel was where Guo wanted to use the elixir to drug prostitutes, but the prostitute who was called was a substitute and could not start. Later, he changed to the Yangzi Hotel, but it was the same. This was the second time that I, Lu, and Li did this illegal thing, but the elixir was still given by Guo. The accusations against Doctor Liu are really false. The rest of the confession was evasive, and Lu Jianying confessed that he was completely harmed by Ruan. He hired two lawyers, Yan Fanggang and Jiang Baoli, to defend him, asking for a lenient sentence so that he could change his ways and start a new life. Li Jianguang confessed that he was also forced by Ruan. Liu Jiaji confessed that he knew nothing about the case. Ruan Zilin has not been to my place for a long time. Please take note. Judge Jiang Shuzi ordered Liu Jiaji to be released on bail, and the rest were returned to prison. The judgment will be announced on the 25th.

Shi Jiurong Nearly Abducted by Bandits - Four Bandits Boarded the Vehicle but Could Not Start It Due to a Secret Switch - A Russian Yelled "Robbers!" and Chinese Police Pursued and Killed One Bandit - Shi Jiurong Has No Assets or Savings 157

Yesterday morning around nine o'clock, at the corner of Avenue Dubail and Avenue du Maréchal Joffre in the French Concession, in front of the American-owned Meitong Automobile Company, the most renowned dealer of Ford and other automobiles in Shanghai, an attempted kidnapping occurred. The intended victim was Shi Jiurong, a mechanic at Meitong. Fortunately, the alertness of his chauffeur, surnamed Rou, and a foreign coppersmith, who shouted for the police, led to the pursuit of the four bandits. One bandit was shot dead on the spot by the police, and the other three escaped. The intended victim managed to escape unharmed. Details are as follows:

Family Background and Occupation

Shi Jiurong, a native of Ningbo, is 32 years old. He graduated from St. John's University in Shanghai and studied in the United States, earning a master's degree in Mechanical Engineering from the University of Michigan. After returning to China, he worked at Xintong Automobile Company on Avenue d'Albert. This year, he transferred from Xintong to Meitong. Shi's family lives at 275 Yuyuan Road in western Shanghai and owns a coffee-colored Buick sedan with license plate number 976 in the International Settlement for transportation, employing a chauffeur named Li Alin.

Bandits Board the Car

Yesterday morning, after getting up and washing and eating, it was already nine o'clock. Shi, considering it was time for work, ordered Li Alin to drive the car out. Shi got into the car, heading straight for the company. However, as soon as the car arrived at the company entrance and the chauffeur stopped the car, Shi was about to reach for the door handle when four bandits suddenly jumped onto the car from behind. Two were dressed in short blue outfits, and two wore long blue robes. Three bandits forced their way into Shi's car compartment, sitting on either side of him and brandishing guns to restrain him.

Unable to Start the Car

The other bandit sat in the front compartment with the chauffeur, Li Alin. He slapped Li twice in the face, ordering him to give up his seat. The bandit then attempted to drive the car himself. However, Li, sensing the danger, had secretly switched off the "hidden starter" beforehand. As a result, when the bandit tried to start the car, the engine could not be started. While the bandits were fumbling in confusion, the doorman-policeman at the company entrance saw Shi's car arrive and calmly approached to open the car door, unaware that there were four bandits inside.

Russian Shouts

But at that moment, when the bandits saw the doorman-policeman approaching, they suspected he was there to arrest them. One of the bandits drew a gun and fired at the policeman, hitting him in the left shin. The gunshot alarmed a Russian coppersmith, Folaike, who was standing nearby. Seeing what was happening, he shouted "Catch the robbers!" in Chinese. The bandits still hoped to succeed and ordered Li Alin to drive quickly, but Li pretended to be unable to. At this point, the bandits realized the situation was hopeless, jumped out of the car, and fled in different directions.

Chinese Police Pursuit

Two bandits fled from Avenue du Maréchal Joffre towards Avenue Joffre, while the other two escaped from Avenue Dubail towards Avenue d'Albert. However, Folaike refused to give up easily and continued to chase and shout. One bandit, in desperation, turned around and fired two shots, but fortunately, both missed. At that moment, a Chinese policeman number 282 from the Public Concession was passing by on a motorcycle. Hearing the shots, he rushed to the scene and joined the pursuit.

One Bandit Killed

The police chased the bandits to the vicinity of Seymour Road and Avenue d'Albert. They saw a bandit running ahead and opened fire. At the same time, Chinese policeman number 349 from the French Concession police also joined in the pursuit. As a result, one bandit was hit by two bullets in the back, which exited through his chest, killing him instantly. The bandit was wearing a long blue robe with a short cotton-padded jacket and black cloth trousers. He was still clutching a handgun tightly in his hand. A large number of detectives from the French Concession police arrived and transported the dead bandit to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall to await examination by the Second Special District Court. Meanwhile, they are investigating to bring his accomplices to justice.

No Assets

According to reporters, Mr. Shi's job at Meitong is mainly to solicit business, in addition to being an engineer. He has no assets or savings. He is usually kind and sincere in his dealings with people and has no enemies. The cause of this incident is probably due to a misunderstanding.

Ningbo Fishing Boat Jin Liyuan Encountered Pirates - Cargo Was Completely Stolen - Accountant Was Abducted - Three Crew Members Killed 160

The Ningbo fishing boat Jin Liyuan recently loaded timber and paper goods in Fuzhou and set sail for Shanghai. On the afternoon of the 14th of this month, when sailing in the waters off Taizhou, it encountered a hurricane and anchored in the port on the south bank of Taizhou to take shelter from the storm. The next morning, the shipowner, Fang Mengrong, instructed the crew not to sail because there were pirates ahead. After the wind and waves subsided, they weighed anchor and sailed. They saw a large three-masted ship approaching. As it drew near, it fired two shots into the air. Fang's ship tried its best to sail, and bamboo bows were placed on both sides of the ship. Unexpectedly, another pirate ship blocked the way, preventing Jin Liyuan from escaping. At that time, four or five of Fang's crew members were injured by bullets. Seeing this, they had to lower the sails and stop. Two pirate ships surrounded them, and the pirates rushed aboard with guns, behaving very aggressively. When they saw the bamboo bows on either side, the pirates became furious and began to beat people indiscriminately and ransack everything. All the silver dollars, crew members' luggage, and bedding were stolen. The timber in the cargo hold was too heavy to steal. Before leaving, they abducted the accountant and fled east. After the pirates left, the owner of Fang's ship saw that most of the crew members were injured and the ship itself was damaged by bullets and could not sail. He hired a tugboat to tow it to Zhenhai, where he sent the injured to the hospital for treatment. Three crew members died from their injuries. Yesterday, Fang took the Xinjin Tianlun steamer to Shanghai and reported the incident to various cargo companies, pleading for the rescue of the abducted accountant.

Escape from Death - Still Unrepentant - Zhang Ziliang Was Once Sentenced to Death - Now Implicated in Another Theft Case 161

Zhang Ziliang, also known as Ma Pi A Kang, a native of Ningbo, is now 41 years old. In 1914, he committed a major crime and was arrested, sent to the former Military Governor's Office, and sentenced to be shot. The sentence was never carried out because of the political upheaval at the time. However, shortly after his release, he was arrested again and sentenced to life imprisonment. He was imprisoned until March 8th, 1925, when he was released. It can be said that he escaped death and should have strived to be a good person. However, on the 19th of last month, the home of Xu Yuchun, who runs a money shop at 10, Lane 232, Qipu Road, was suddenly robbed by a group of armed bandits. Afterwards, Detective Shang Wu of the Huisibang Police Station arrested eleven bandits and seized four handguns. According to the bandits, Zhang Ziliang was also an accomplice and supplied them with firearms. Detective Shang immediately purchased a lead to arrest Zhang. On the night of the 17th, at 9 PM, he learned that Zhang was hiding in room 514 of the Dahua Hotel on Xizang Road. He rushed to the scene with detectives and captured Zhang. However, Zhang vehemently denied colluding with others to rob with weapons. Yesterday morning, the police escorted Zhang to the First Special District Court and brought the previously arrested bandits to court for questioning. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu stated that Zhang had not admitted to the robbery, and the police still needed to investigate, so they could not prosecute Zhang yet. He requested temporary detention and further investigation before prosecution. Judge Liu then questioned the bandit who claimed Zhang was an accomplice. The bandit suddenly said that he had previously borrowed money from Zhang but was rejected, so he made false accusations out of spite, and now he felt he should not have done so. Zhang still denied being a thief. The victim, Xu Yuchun, hired lawyer Ge Zhaoji to appear in court, requesting that the bandits be severely punished. Judge Liu ruled that the case still needed to be investigated, so he ordered that all parties be returned to custody and the hearing be rescheduled.
