Easter Holiday - Foreign Banks Closed for Three Days 166

Today is Easter (commonly known as the Foreign Qingming Festival). According to custom, foreign banks and firms on the Bund are closed for three days. Since the holiday falls on a Sunday, April 21st, the following day will be a make-up holiday. As such, they will only reopen on Tuesday, April 23rd, resulting in a four-day closure. Among Chinese banks, only China, Jiaotong, and Tongshang Banks will follow the old custom of closing. The rest will operate as usual. It is said that the Central Bank and Customs will not be participating.

Closing of the Pro-Life Art Exhibition 167

The Pro-Life art exhibition organized by the Shanghai-based Western Association for the Prevention of Cruelty to Animals has been well received by the public since its opening on the 11th of this month. Many people have visited. Yesterday (the 17th) was the closing date, and the number of visitors was even more numerous. It evokes compassion. It is said that the association's award plan is to award commendations and certificates in grades A, B, and C to all schools and individuals who participate in the works. Schools and individuals who win the top three places will receive valuable prizes. The China Animal Protection Association will issue a notice to collect these prizes, and the preparations are actively underway.

Police Officer Killed by Truck on Zhongshan Road - Autopsy Completed Yesterday, Funeral Today 171

It was reported in yesterday's newspaper that at around 5 PM the day before yesterday, Zhu Jishan (police number 1979) of the Tanzibang Police Station of the Zhabei Police Bureau was hit and injured by a truck while on duty at the intersection of Zhongshan Road and Jiaotong Road. He was sent to a hospital in the concession, where he died at around 8 PM that night. According to reports, the corpse was escorted to the morgue at 9 AM yesterday by Inspector Li Qingjie of the Tanzibang Police Station, and the First Special District Court was requested to perform an autopsy. The prosecutor arrived at 2 PM to perform the autopsy. The body was brought back to Zhabei by Inspector Li. The deceased's original residence was at Hengqiao Lane, Hengqiao Road, where the landlord would not allow the body to be placed in the house, so it was temporarily placed in an open space at the entrance of Faxiang Lane on Datong Road. A canopy was quickly built. Ruan Kai-mu, chief of the Xinzha Police Bureau, sold the canopy, purchased a coffin, and prepared for the burial this morning. The deceased originally worked for the Finance Bureau there before being transferred to the Tanzibang Police Station only two weeks ago. He is survived by a wife, Wang, 22 years old, and a son named Jin, who is a few months old.

Postman's Extreme Misconduct - Stealing Stamps and Destroying Letters - More Than Sixty Letters Found on Him at Once - A Large Number of Letters Were Also Found in His Home 172

Dong Jianyuan, a native of Shandong, who lives at 271 Fuli Road in the French Concession, is 33 years old and works as mailman number 807 at the 18th Postal District branch in Shanghai. He used to be a mailman at the Harbin Post Office in the Northeast. After the Northeast fell, he was transferred to Tianjin and finally to Shanghai. He has been serving in the post office for five or six years. He earns 53 yuan a month, collecting mail from mailboxes on various roads. Recently, due to financial difficulties, he had a wild idea. When collecting mail from post boxes on various roads every day, he secretly took out several or dozens of letters. He would peel off the stamps on the letters and sell them for money, and then tear up and discard the letters from which the stamps had been removed, thinking that no one would know. However, recently, people have often come to the post office to inquire about undelivered letters, so the bureau ordered a secret investigation. At around 6 PM the other afternoon, investigator No. 2 found Dong collecting letters from the post box at Shengmuyuan Bridge on Xujiahui Road in the French Concession. The investigator saw that Dong was hiding the letters he collected from the post box in his own pocket, so he stepped forward to question him. Dong's face turned red, and he was unable to answer. The investigator then found nearly 60 letters in his pocket and arrested Dong along with the stolen letters. Detective Zhang Daorong and Bao Detective Shen Jinshi took Dong to his home to search and found a large number of letters, which they brought back to the police station. Yesterday, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. Judge Qiu Huan-ying presided over the trial. Police lawyer Gu Shouxi explained the case and prosecuted him for dereliction of duty and theft. The plaintiff, the representative of the Postal Administration, and the witness, investigator So-and-so, stated the process of discovering and catching the defendant. When questioned, Dong admitted to stealing stamps and destroying letters. The court verified the confession and ruled that the case still needed to be investigated, so they ordered the hearing to be rescheduled for May 4th. The defendant was returned to custody.

Another Youth Commits Suicide 176

On the evening of April 16th, a young man arrived at the Qinghua Hotel at 9, Lane 352, Shandong Road, booked room 17, paid the room fee, and wrote his name as Li Lin, from Qingpu, 31 years old, in the register. It is not known what caused him to have a pessimistic thought and secretly took poison. Around 2 PM the next day, the hotel waiter, Wang A-fu, went to ask if he would like to extend his stay, as usual. He found the door was locked and knocked but received no response. He suspected something was wrong and tried to open the door. He found the guest moaning on the bed, his face pale. He called the Old Zha Criminal Police Station and a rescue vehicle was summoned to rush him to Renji Hospital. Efforts to save him were ineffective, and he soon died. The police station dispatched Chinese detectives to investigate. A suicide note was found near the deceased's body, addressed to the hotel, which read: "I am committing suicide in your hotel because I am suffering from a bad environment, mental confusion, and a lack of interest in life. I came to Shanghai this afternoon without saying goodbye to my family. I leave behind a watch and $1.60, which should be given to Mr. Yao." The police then took the body to the Pei Lun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Tang, the prosecutor assigned by the First Special District Court, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. Chinese officer Xue Ziweng reported the situation, saying that he could not find any relatives or friends of the deceased and asked for instructions. Wang Afu also described the situation at the time. Tang ruled that the deceased, Li Lin, was a male and died from poisoning. Since there were no family members, the body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial. The items left behind were sent to the hospital by the police station to await collection.

Arrest of Snake-Skin Jinlan's Followers 177

Chen Jinlan, a Yong native and murder suspect nicknamed "Snake-Skin Jinlan," who was detained in the Second Special District Local Court Detention Center, escaped from prison between 3:00 AM and 7:00 AM on November 27th of last year. He fled to Hankou, but unable to make a living, recently snuck back to Shanghai and hid in the home of his fellow villager Bian Wuchang, located on the front building of the wood shop at No. 32 Lao Yong'an Street in the French Concession. Detectives Lu Dongliang and Yang Zhongfang of the French Concession Police learned of this, and on the afternoon of the 15th, they secretly went to the address and arrested Chen. They also arrested Bian Wuchang for the crime of harboring a criminal, and both were transferred to the Second Special Court for interrogation and investigation. This was detailed in a previous report. It is now known that during the investigation, the detectives found that Wang Afu (age 21, from Suzhou), a vendor residing at No. 44, Jiuyuan Lane, Yalu Road, Hongkou, was Chen Jinlan's follower. Last month, Chen encountered Wang near Nan Chu's Bridge on Mintini Road and borrowed money from him. Wang agreed and borrowed money from others to give to Chen for his use and concealment. It was determined that Wang was also suspected of jointly harboring a criminal. Therefore, at around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, Wang was arrested at the entrance of Shangxian Lane on Xiafei Road, taken back to the police station, and detained. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. Attorney Yuan Jiahuan of the police station presented the case and requested a postponement to combine it with the Chen Jinlan case for investigation. Judge Li Changnian briefly questioned Wang and then ordered a postponement to the 26th to be tried together with Chen Jinlan. The defendant was returned to custody.

276th Preparation Report Issued by the Four Banks Joint Treasury 180

The Four Banks Joint Treasury is jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu banks to handle the issuance of Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the treasury's issuance regulations, banknotes are issued with full reserves, with cash reserves accounting for at least 60% and guaranteed reserves accounting for up to 40%. A public announcement is made every week, and it is reviewed by auditors and accountants from the four banks. The 276th announcement of the Shanghai Treasury as of April 13, 1935, is recorded below: Amount of banknotes in circulation: 22,185,672 yuan. Total reserves: 22,185,673 yuan. Significant Progress in the Smallpox Vaccination Work of the Municipal Council's Health Department: Over 90,000 People Vaccinated in March 182

According to a report from the Municipal Council's Health Department, the smallpox vaccination work in March of this year was unexpectedly successful. A total of 93,306 people were vaccinated throughout the month. On March 16th alone, the day of the Flower Festival, as many as 25,930 people were vaccinated. This year, cases of smallpox have been almost non-existent, and the public's enthusiasm for vaccination is a welcome phenomenon. The work on the Flower Festival day was largely due to the assistance of Chinese and foreign volunteers, which made it possible to create an unprecedented record. In the past, medical officers in the concession put a lot of effort into promoting vaccination. In 1870, the Municipal Council established free vaccination facilities, and the Shanghai Daotai also issued a notice prohibiting the old method of vaccination. In 1894, the Municipal Council established a smallpox vaccination branch, which was also greatly supported by the Chinese officials. However, because the method of compulsion relied only on persuasion, progress was very slow. As of 19--, only 4,600 people were vaccinated by the Health Department throughout the year. Compared with recent years, when over 200,000 people are vaccinated each year, the difference is significant.

Since 1910, a total of 1,435,000 people have been vaccinated with cowpox by the Health Department. A large amount of vaccine has also been distributed to various hospitals and charitable organizations. Therefore, it is estimated that over 2.5 million people have been protected from smallpox. However, given the high mobility of Shanghai's population, the risk of infection still exists at any time, so it is necessary to continue to work hard on vaccination.

The Popularity of "The Death of Lingyu" 183

The performance of "The Death of Lingyu" at the Gong Stage is a real-life drama that has caused a social sensation no less than the "Yan Ruisheng" case performed at the New Stage more than ten years ago. The play uses both gongs and drums and piano and phonograph, opening up a new path between Peking opera and spoken drama. In terms of scenery, places such as Kunshan Garden, Taikoo Wharf, Qinyuan Village, Great Light Cinema, Sino-Western Sanatorium, and International Funeral Home are as realistic as the real scenes. Tong Yuejuan plays Zhang Zhiyun, Han Suqiu plays Ruan Lingyu, Chuan Xiaobo plays Tang Jishan, and Xia Yinpei plays Zhang Damin, all imitating their spirit and demeanor with eight or nine points of similarity. Therefore, since its premiere, it has been performed for half a month, and the popularity has not diminished. This shows the extent to which the play is welcomed by the public.

National Trust Bank Adds Treasury Bond Custody Method: The Savings Department of the National Trust Bank on Sanma Road in this city has recently noted that the various treasury bonds issued by the government have increasing creditworthiness and stable prices, occupying the center of social finance. The number of ordinary people who rely on them for their livelihoods as fixed assets is huge. However, collecting principal and interest every month is crowded and troublesome. Therefore, it has specially added the custody of various treasury bonds, collecting principal and interest on their behalf, and savings deposits are divided into four types of custody. Collection is free of charge, and the interest rate is high. The highest interest rate can reach 1.25% per month. According to the recent market price of the 22-year Customs Treasury Bonds, storing principal and interest in the bank for 15 years will yield approximately seven times the cash. This is truly good news for the public and bondholders. It is heard that it will start on the 25th of this month.

Medical and Pharmaceutical Circles 191

Asthma-Relieving Esmorelle: The Swiss Ruikang Foreign Company at No. 133 Yuanmingyuan Road in this city has recently handled a type of asthma medicine called Esmorelle. This medicine was invented by Dr. Ers and has long been popular worldwide. Many major doctors in our country also use it as a specific drug to treat asthma, and long-term use has the effect of treating the root cause. It is divided into two types: injection and tablets. Injections are for use when asthma attacks occur and can be used by major doctors in clinical practice. Tablets are for long-term use after an attack and can prevent the recurrence of asthma. It is truly good news for those who suffer from this disease. This medicine is sold in major pharmacies. Detailed instructions are available upon request.

Letters to the Editor 193

To the Editor: Yesterday, I read a news report in your newspaper's local section entitled "Gamblers Fight and Stab Each Other Six Times, Life in Danger," which mentioned my father and son, Wu Jinsheng and Wu Jiren. After investigation, this case is completely based on revenge and false accusations (omitted). In addition to my father and son legally filing a request with the court to investigate and clarify the truth, the newspaper reports do not conform to the facts and concern the business reputation of our store. We have specially provided a brief account of the facts and respectfully request that it be published in the Letters to the Editor section to correct and maintain our reputation. In the future, after the court investigates this case, the truth will not be difficult to reveal. Respectfully, Senyuantai Coal Store, Longquanyuan Hot Water Store, April 17.

To the Editor: Sir, today your newspaper's news section carried an item about the British Commercial Kwong Company reducing rent. After investigation, our company has not reduced rent in the Pengpu Road area. Only a few Western houses in the Diswei Road area have been reduced because the trust households in that area have not recovered to their original state since the January 28th Incident. As for Hengfeng Lane on Wusong Road, it is not our company's property. We are afraid that there will be misunderstandings, so we have specially written to your newspaper to correct the matter and request that it be published in the Letters to the Editor section. Sincerely, British Commercial Kwong Real Estate Company, April 18.

Educational News Special Issue

National Revival and the Reading Movement 196

— Chen Lifu

—Opening Address of the National Reading Movement Congress—

The Chinese Cultural Construction Association held the National Reading Movement Congress from April 8th to 21st. Mr. Chen Lifu, the chairman of the association, requested Mr. Zhang Daofan, a director, to broadcast the opening address of the National Reading Movement Congress at 8:00 AM on April 8th at the Nanjing Central Broadcasting Station. The main points of his speech were instructed by Mr. Lifu. Afterwards, his speech was edited and published. The full text is as follows:

Gentlemen, today is the first day of the National Reading Movement Congress organized by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association. I would like to report the important significance of holding this National Reading Movement Congress to all the beloved comrades and compatriots across the country. We all deeply feel the precariousness of the nation's position and the perilousness of the national situation. We believe that at this critical moment, the national revival movement is the self-awareness, self-confidence, and self-striving that every citizen should possess. In recent years, the central government's measures in military affairs, politics, party affairs, and education have all stemmed from this major premise of the national revival movement. However, we firmly believe that the strength or weakness, prosperity or decline of a nation is entirely based on whether its culture is flourishing or not. Therefore, on the eve of the national revival movement, we should have a vigorous and practical cultural revival movement. We should use the cultural revival movement to lay a deep and solid foundation for the national revival movement. Moreover, only if the cultural revival movement succeeds can the national revival movement not be empty talk and can it be realized as scheduled.

If we want to revive our culture, we must first have a prerequisite. This prerequisite is how to restore the nation's confidence in building culture. If the general public does not have confidence in building culture, then it is truly the so-called "nothing is more sorrowful than a dead heart." What hope is there to speak of? The so-called self-confidence means having something within oneself. To explain it more practically, it means first having self-awareness. The old problem of the Chinese people is that they either exaggerate themselves or belittle themselves. This problem of excess and deficiency is the biggest reason why the Chinese nation cannot make progress. In terms of culture, those who exaggerate themselves advocate extreme restoration of the old, while those who belittle themselves advocate complete Westernization. These two extreme views not only do not benefit Chinese culture but are likely to lead our country into an even more chaotic and dark situation. Therefore, our attitude towards reviving national culture should be neither blindly exaggerating nor blindly belittling ourselves, but rather taking the spirit of self-reliance and self-help, learning from others' strengths, and making up for our own weaknesses to build a world's healthiest new culture. At the same time, we must do our best to contribute to others to demonstrate the inherent characteristics of our nation.

In order to achieve the above-mentioned goals, we should determine our attitude towards the past, present, and future. In the history of the world, our country's cultural brilliance has been unparalleled. This is an undeniable fact. Stretching tens of thousands of miles and spanning thousands of years, there have been countless sages and heroes who have displayed their intelligence and built their careers, winning glory for the Chinese nation. However, in the past hundred years, due to material inferiority and lack of self-defense, we have repeatedly failed in foreign wars, and national rights and interests have been lost day by day. As a result, the general public has embarked on a path of decadence and discouragement, thinking that China is inferior to others in everything and that the legacy passed down by our ancestors is not worth cherishing. In fact, this is a major fallacy. We must know that our intelligence and ability are not inferior to any excellent nation, and the elaboration and creation of various academic systems in history cannot be erased by anyone. Therefore, for the sake of establishing a brand-new and healthy culture for the nation, we should not adopt a purely dismissive attitude towards the past culture. We should actively use scientific methods to sort out all the cultural relics accumulated by the inherent intelligence of our ancestors, taking what should be taken and discarding what should be discarded. Only after the inherent culture has been sorted out by scientific methods can it be sifted like gold from sand, becoming useful, radiant, and inexhaustible.

The reason why our country is in a semi-colonial position today has its historical causes and is also due to the psychological suicide of some of our people. Because the establishment of a sound culture emphasizes both the development of spiritual culture and the creation of material culture. Our past culture emphasized spiritual aspects, while European and American culture emphasized material aspects. Therefore, after the contact between China and the West, Western guns and cannons destroyed the ancient Great Wall. Our country suffered loss of power and territory due to material inferiority, and was marked by shame. Assuming that the general public could have realized this early, studied the points of failure, and strived for self-salvation, then the history of China in the past hundred years would not have been scarred to this day. The most heartbreaking thing is that since the Opium War, Chinese intellectuals have lost their self-confidence, and the entire Chinese nation has lost the treasure of self-confidence, which is the foundation of a nation. As a result, the wheels of time have moved forward relentlessly, only creating a situation where our country is getting worse and worse. Our culture's emphasis on the development of the spiritual aspect is a historical cause, but the Chinese people's loss of the treasure of self-confidence is a psychological suicide. What about Chinese intellectuals now? Are they aware? Many people are still living a romantic life in a passive and decadent way, taking a cold and detached attitude towards the rise and fall of the nation and the survival of the country. They do not recognize the root of the nation's and country's illness, nor do they see through the path that modern Chinese society needs to strive for. If everyone is like this, how can China have hope? Therefore, we must not hold a passive and detached attitude. We should restore national self-confidence and recognize that modern China, lacking material culture, needs scientific knowledge to enrich it and improve the level of social culture.

We can thoroughly sort out the past culture, and we can thoroughly enrich the current needs, saving the dying nation from the root, but we must not be satisfied with this. We must know that the life of the nation, we should not only fulfill the responsibility of maintaining it, and prolonging its life, but also promote and develop it for the sake of the whole world and all mankind. If we want to achieve this great goal and fulfill this sacred mission, we must use the scientific spirit to promote and develop the life of the nation, use scientific methods to sort out everything in the past, use scientific knowledge to enrich everything in the present, and use scientific spirit to create everything in the future. These are the three major tasks of the Chinese cultural revival movement, and the three major routes for building Chinese national culture. To complete this review, (organize the past, grasp (enrich) the present, and create the future, we should start from (1) being studious, (2) striving to act, and (3) knowing shame.

Being studious means competing with others in intelligence. The modern world is a world of intellectual competition. The intellectually strong win, and the intellectually weak lose. There is no luck in the way of survival. If we want to use scientific methods to sort out everything in the past, use scientific knowledge to enrich everything in the present, and use the scientific spirit to develop everything in the future, we must deal with it with great intelligence. Intelligence training and cultivation lie in being studious. Striving to act means competing with others in ability. The Chinese people have long been poisoned by the idea that "it is not difficult to know, but it is difficult to act." The reason why we have failed in everything and accomplished nothing is that we cannot strive to act. Therefore, we should strive to act with the spirit of Mr. Sun Yat-sen that it is easy to act and difficult to know. The way to revive culture lies in this, and the way to revive the nation also lies in this. Knowing shame means making up for the lack of knowledge and ability in order to prepare for avenging shame. As the saying goes, "Knowing shame is close to courage." If we have the self-awareness of knowing shame, we should have the preparation for avenging shame. The preparation for avenging shame lies in making up for the lack of intelligence. Therefore, being able to make up for the lack of intelligence is clear evidence of knowing shame. If everyone can be studious, then what foreigners know, we will all know. If everyone can strive to act, then what foreigners can do, we will all be able to do. If everyone knows shame, then their intelligence will be sufficient, national shame can be avenged at any time, and the national foundation can be revived at any time. If every person can be down-to-earth and earnestly do these three things: "being studious," "striving to act," and "knowing shame," I firmly believe that the success of the cultural revival movement and the success of the national revival movement are just around the corner.

Youth is the soul of the country and the backbone of the nation. The strength of the country and the prosperity or decline of the nation are determined by the will of the youth and the direction of their efforts. We only hope that the youth who are studying now will make full use of their time in school, and the youth who are working will make full use of their spare time. Not only youth, but also children, adults, and the elderly, can all strive to do these three things: "being studious," "striving to act," and "knowing shame." Then, there will be no problem in promoting and developing the Chinese nation and creating a first-class civilized country in the world. The significance of the Reading Progress Competition held by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association and the National Reading Movement Congress held from today onwards lies in our greatest hope and highest enthusiasm that all comrades and compatriots across the country will participate in this reading movement and achieve the goal of "saving the Chinese nation from the root and working hard to meet the challenge."

In view of the perilousness of the nation's position, empty talk of saving the country is ineffective. The great cause of saving the country does not lie in empty talk but in practice. Moreover, we should start from ourselves. Starting from ourselves is the most practical and easiest way. Scholars should intensify their studies, farmers should intensify production, workers should improve their skills, and businessmen should promote domestic goods. Each should start from their own position and work hard. China will certainly have infinite hope. At the same time, we should pay more attention to the fact that the progress of agriculture, industry, and commerce will not be successful without the increase of scholars' knowledge. Because the increase of rural production, the progress of industrial skills, and the development of businessmen's patriotism are all important goals of education and the greatest goals of the reading movement.

To give a simple example, everyone knows that future wars will be three-dimensional wars, and the air force will occupy a decisive position in future battles. Therefore, in recent years, the entire country has been committed to saving the country through aviation. However, the content of the two words "aviation" includes many specialized knowledge. Taking the manufacturing of an aircraft as an example, it requires mechanical engineering, electrical engineering, mining and metallurgical engineering, chemical engineering, textile engineering, etc. The construction of the airport and the lighting equipment require the design of civil engineering and physics and chemistry experts. Saving the country through aviation certainly requires economy and financial resources, but what is even more needed is manpower and academic ability. Can we save the country by simply buying hundreds or thousands of aircraft from foreign countries? Only when we can manufacture and fly aircraft ourselves can we talk about saving the country through aviation. If we hope to manufacture it ourselves, we need to read books and study science. Who doesn't know the bankruptcy of Chinese rural areas? Who doesn't know that if we don't save the rural areas, China will perish soon? However, can saving the rural areas be done through empty talk? Everything requires real measures. Therefore, at this critical moment, we should be down-to-earth, earnestly do our work, and meet the urgent needs of the country and the nation.

For the needs of national defense and production, the Chinese Cultural Construction Association has organized a reading progress competition and held a National Reading Movement Congress, hoping that all comrades and compatriots across the country will understand this important significance, practice it personally, and know that enriching one's own academic ability is enriching the strength of the nation, and building one's own intelligence is building the culture of the nation. When the cultural revival movement is completed, it will be the day when the cornerstone of the national revival movement is laid. The end.

The Number and Subject of Students Studying Abroad in Our Country in the Recent Five Years 203

The Ministry of Education has compiled statistics on the number and subjects of students sent to various countries in the past years up to the 21st year. Now, based on the investigation, combined with the recent situation, a statistics on the number and subjects of students studying abroad in the recent five years is made as follows:

(A) The number of students studying abroad in the recent five years is: (1) European countries (including France, Germany, England, Belgium, Austria) 356 in the 18th year, 266 in the 19th year, 241 in the 20th year, 241 in the 21st year, and 208 in the 22nd year; (2) American countries (including the United States and Canada) 272 in the 18th year, 158 in the 19th year, 118 in the 20th year, 100 in the 21st year, and 187 in the 22nd year; (3) Other countries (including Japan, Sweden, Italy, Switzerland, Egypt, the Philippines, India) 1029 in the 18th year, 606 in the 19th year, 90 in the 20th year, 235 in the 21st year, and 226 in the 22nd year; (B) The subjects of students studying abroad in the recent five years (1) Europe, America, Japan, and other countries, in the 18th year, 568 studied law and politics, 249 studied engineering, 26 studied literature and philosophy, 104 studied medicine, 129 studied science, 75 studied education, 66 studied agriculture and forestry, 62 studied commerce, 9 studied military affairs, and 129 were not specified (a total of 1657); (2) In the 19th year, 307 studied law and politics, 165 studied engineering, 166 studied literature and philosophy, 109 studied medicine, 77 studied science, 56 studied education, 49 studied agriculture and forestry, 43 studied commerce, and 58 were not specified (a total of 1030); (3) In the 20th year, 108 studied law and politics, 79 studied engineering, 57 studied literature and philosophy, 60 studied medicine, 64 studied science, 45 studied education, 17 studied agriculture and forestry, 11 studied commerce, and 9 were not specified (450); (4) In the 21st year, 49 studied science, 35 studied agriculture and forestry, 76 studied engineering, 53 studied medicine, 98 studied literature and art, 179 studied law and politics, 40 studied education, 25 studied commerce, and 12 were not specified (a total of 576); (5) In the 22nd year, 55 studied science, 40 studied agriculture and forestry, 139 studied engineering, 83 studied medicine, 78 studied literature and art, 151 studied law and politics, 45 studied education, 27 studied commerce, and 3 were not specified (a total of 621); (C) The number in the 23rd year is temporarily calculated as two-thirds, (the 23rd year will only end at the end of June of this year, so we will calculate based on the eight months that have passed by two-thirds, up to the end of February of this year,) a total of 409 students have studied in Europe, America, Japan, and other countries, of which Japan has the most with 213, followed by the United States, followed by the United Kingdom, and Canada and Switzerland have the least. The subjects are 206 in liberal arts (including literature, art, law, politics, education, and commerce) and 203 in science (including science, agriculture, forestry, engineering, and medicine).

Zhang Sumin Speaks on How to Study Economics 204

Yesterday was the tenth day of the National Reading Movement Congress organized by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association. The association specially invited Dr. Zhang Sumin, Director of the Banking Department of National Jinan University, to speak on how to study economics. The following is a transcript of the speech:

Today, I am honored to be invited by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association to speak on the topic of "How to Study Economics." I will share my humble views with you.

The Importance of Economics Economic life occupies the largest part of human life. The so-called economic life includes all activities such as the production, distribution, exchange, and consumption of wealth. Farms, factories, shops, offices, transportation agencies, etc., are the locations of production and distribution. All buying and selling belong to exchange, and clothing, food, housing, and transportation, etc., belong to consumption. We rise at the crowing of the rooster and go out to work or office, wanting to serve production and distribute a portion so that we can exchange it for other things to satisfy the desire for consumption. Although I am not a proponent of the monistic economic history view, I cannot but admit the great influence of economic life on other aspects of life. The Confucians have the saying that one should enrich the people first and then teach them. Guanzi has the theory of sufficient clothing and food, and full granaries. It can be seen that our ancient sages had already seen this. Economics is the science of studying economic life, and its importance is self-evident. In addition, modern economic situations are becoming increasingly complex, and to understand them clearly, we rely more on the study of economics.

The Object of Economics In the past, scholars thought that economics was only the science of studying human activities such as acquiring wealth and using wealth. They recognized that the object of economics was wealth, etc. Modern scholars think that economics is the science of studying the relationship between people caused by activities such as acquiring wealth and using wealth and how to increase people's happiness. Therefore, they recognize that the object of economics is happiness. For example, when we study the Chinese economy, we should not only focus on developing production and raising the level of consumption, but also focus on how developing production can benefit the common people and how it can raise the level of consumption and increase the happiness of the common people.

Methods of Entry The methods of entry to study economics can be divided into two types: one is to study the basic principles of economics, and the other is to study practical economic problems. If you want to study the basic principles, you should start with textbooks. Those who can read Western texts can choose a "standard textbook," such as Ely's "Outlines of Economics" or Bye's "Principles of Economics." Those who read Chinese texts can choose to read Wang Jianzu's translation of "Kitt's Economics" or Chen Jiazan's translation of "Tsumura Hidematsu's Economics." After reading a book carefully and referring to two or three books, you can know the general outline of the basic principles. As for studying practical economic problems, such as those concerning the world, you can read a book on "Economic Problems" in Western languages. There are many books of this kind in Western languages, and you can choose one. As for those concerning China, there are very few books of this kind. As far as I know, Mr. Ma Yinchu's new book "The Reconstruction of the Chinese Economy" has detailed discussions on various important economic problems in China. It can be called the first book on "Chinese Economic Problems." The "Business Report of the 23rd Year" recently published by the Bank of China speaks clearly about the economic situation last year. In addition, we should pay attention to the economic news and essays published in Chinese and Western newspapers and magazines. As long as we pay attention, we can study less data anytime and anywhere.

Specialized Research Each topic included in an economics book can be used as a lifelong specialized research, such as currency, banking, labor, transportation, distribution, consumption, management, and other items, all of which can be studied with a lifetime of effort. Those who love to study ideological theories can also make the history of world economic thought a major topic. We can choose a topic according to our own interests and do in-depth specialized research.

Application of Theory We study economics not only for "intellectual exercise." We should seek to solve problems. Former scholars divided economics into "pure economics" and "applied economics," thinking that the former is the study of principles and the latter is the solution of problems. In fact, this kind of classification is modeled on natural sciences. In terms of economics, this kind of classification is not very appropriate. The principle of economics is the principle of discussing problems. If the principle cannot solve the problem, it loses the qualification of the principle. We should seek to discover new principles in the study of problems. Therefore, after we have a clear understanding of all existing principles, we should consider the environment and temporarily propose a plan for the solution of practical problems. The basis of the proposed plan may be the old principles or the new principles determined by the integration of the old principles and according to the environment of the problem. To achieve this level, we must study deeply and have rich insights.

Municipal People's Education Center to Hold Children's Storytelling Contest; Registration Begins Today, Limited to 30 Participants; To be Held at the Center at 9 AM on April 28th 208

The Shanghai Municipal People's Education Center will hold a children's storytelling contest at the center at 9:00 AM on the 28th of this month. Registration begins today. The contest rules and procedures are listed below:

Contest Rules: (1) The purpose of this event is to inspire children's storytelling talent and enhance their thinking ability. (2) All children aged 8 to 14, regardless of gender, may participate in the contest after being approved by the center and issued a competition certificate. (3) The center's competition procedures will be determined separately. (4) The storytelling material must not involve superstition or mythology. (5) The center will hire a number of judges for the competition to evaluate based on the following criteria: A. Structure 40%, B. Posture 30%, C. Tone 30%. (6) The top five winners of the competition will be rewarded by the center. (7) These rules shall be implemented upon approval by the center's administrative meeting.

Contest Procedures: The contest procedures are as follows: (1) The number of participants is limited to 30. (2) The competition date is April 28th, starting at 9:00 AM. (3) The competition venue is the center's lecture hall. (4) The competition time is limited to a maximum of 5 minutes per person. (5) The order of competition will be determined by drawing lots. (6) The registration location is the center's second office. (7) The registration date is from today until the quota is full.

Minutes of the Shanghai Branch Meeting of the Chinese Chemical Society 211

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Chemical Society held a regular meeting at the International Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road on the 14th at noon. More than 50 members attended, including Xu Peihuang, Wu Yunxu, Shen Xiongqing, Zeng Guangfang, Chen Taosheng, Xu Mingcai, Zhang Weiru, Tang Yuanji, Xu Zuohe, Shao Jialin, Yu Xueyang, Wu Haoran, and Zheng Lanhua. After the meal, Shen Xiongqing stood up to give a speech, briefly stating that the chairman of the Shanghai Branch, Mr. Wang Jiliang, had gone abroad for inspection last year and has not yet returned. This regular meeting was convened by himself (the Shanghai Branch was established not long ago, and the number of members has increased from 35 to over 100. The new members are all well-known figures in the chemical field. The addition of this new force will surely bring good suggestions for the development of the association, and it is hoped that they will be submitted to himself at any time). Next, Dr. Ma Bide, a physiological chemistry expert who recently returned from England, was introduced to give a lecture on "New Developments in Vitamin A." Dr. Ma has extensive research on vitamin problems. He gave a very detailed explanation of the discovery, preparation, chemical composition, molecular structure, and urgent technical problems to be solved regarding Vitamin A. Dr. Ma also reported that he is studying the amount of Vitamin A contained in more than 300 medicinal materials in the Compendium of Materia Medica that can treat night blindness and comparing their advantages and disadvantages for the reference of medical practitioners.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 226

— (Reclining Buddha)

It is indeed not easy to be a person in society. Not easy, of course, means "difficult." Divided and classified, there are three types of difficulty in being a person: one is "difficult to be a person," one is "being a difficult person," and one is "being a person is difficult."

"Difficult to be a person" - living in such a society with an increasingly high standard of living, especially under the economic downturn, one must not only shoulder the heavy burden of supporting elders and raising children, but also deal with the social obligations of relatives and friends. For such a person, is it difficult or not?

"Being a difficult person" - you are motivated by patriotic enthusiasm to engage in national salvation movements, but people say you are too radical, even saying you are reactionary; but if you put the rise and fall of the country out of your mind and do not express yourself, people will say that you have no national concept. There are many other similar situations. For such a person, is it difficult or not?

"Being a person is difficult" - as a person, one should do some beneficial things for society and make some contributions to the country. But this requires both knowledge and opportunity. Without this knowledge and opportunity, your life is in vain, failing the country, failing society, and failing yourself. For such a person, is it difficult or not?

However, there is no "difficult" word in Napoleon's dictionary. We must also break through this "difficult" word!

An Analysis of Aspects of the City 227

— Zhou Yimin

The weather is so muggy that it almost makes everyone sleepy. Although spring has arrived, it seems that everyone is going to the countryside to be active. However, upon closer thought, it is just a magnification of sleeping.

"Spring sleep doesn't realize dawn, everywhere you hear birds chirping." In the big city, there is no such elegant sleep as in poetry. After all, every morning, it is always so noisy, and it also makes everyone go to the street to taste the smell of feces. The sound of the chamber pot rustling is like the prelude to a stinky song.

Moreover, the dust on the road is always rolling with the trams and cars, rolling onto everyone's body, rolling into everyone's mouth, rolling into everyone's eyes... Mr. Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, once said that when walking on the streets of Shanghai, you must remember to lock your mouth tightly. If you open it, you will eat dust, and maybe you will eat various infectious diseases.

On the outside, everything looks good, but at heart, it's a mess. You see many people are working for the welfare of the public, but if you look at them with a microscope, their starting point is all about making more money.

All kinds of experts are showing off. Their business is particularly prosperous in this otherwise depressed economy. They fool around with this and that, making some stupid people like ants on a hot pot. They are willing to be fooled.

Enough, enough, no need to write more. Let's write this article for self-praise and praise of others.

A Record of Viewing the Relics of the Pingquan Study 228

— Zheng Yimei

Mr. Li Pingshu, whose name is recorded in the Party history, has been dead for many years. Mr. Li had an elegant temperament. All his salary was used to buy paintings and calligraphy of the past, which he enjoyed playing with in his bright window, taking it as a pleasure. At that time, the famous painter and calligrapher Mr. Wang Nianci participated in Mr. Li's literary circle, and there was hardly a day when he didn't identify and comment on the works. People in the country all knew that the collection of Pingquan Study was rich and abundant, and its accumulation was vast, making it unattainable. Pingquan Study was the name of Mr. Li's studio. Mr. Li's grandson, Xiangfu, loved paintings and calligraphy as much as his grandfather. He treasured them as precious objects. Recently, Mr. Wang Nianci has been setting up his studio on the top floor of Qiugu Zhai on Third Ma Road. The crystal windows are bright and clear, providing a great joy of painting and calligraphy. Mr. Xiangfu, for the convenience of airing the books, wished to display them in the studio for the public to view. Nianci was an old friend of mine, and he invited me to view the works. There were two or three hundred paintings and calligraphies. The most precious one was a huge landscape painting by Huang Gongwang, which had been transported to Tokyo in the past, and people in the East unanimously praised it. It won an award and returned. Looking at it, the spirit is mellow and appropriate, and the brush and ink are noble and pure, which is indeed something that people of the time could not dream of. It is truly a feast for the eyes! Emperor Huizong of Song's painting of an eagle, in its golden splendor, has a magnificent and vigorous atmosphere, making it an especially precious and rare item. The rarest ones are the calligraphy works of Wang Yuyang and Yuan Suiyuan. We usually recite their poems and essays, and once we see their genuine works, how can our longing hearts restrain themselves? In addition to calligraphy and painting, Nianci is also proficient in the art of physiognomy. Among the books on physiognomy, he considers the seven chapters of Bingjian to be the most refined and insightful. The name of the author of this book is not mentioned, making it a secret manual. Zeng Guofan of Xiangxiang highly praised this chapter, calling it the standard of physiognomy and a book that must be read. Nianci accidentally obtained a copy of it, but it was half-eaten by bookworms, so he personally proofread it and recorded the entire chapter, storing it in lithography to prevent it from being lost. He generously presented me with a copy. The so-called seven chapters are: one, spirit and bones; two, firmness and softness; three, appearance; four, emotion; five, eyebrows and beard; six, voice; and seven, complexion. Even in terms of literary expression, it is elegant and readable, washing away the vulgar habits. Kuai Tong looking at the back, Xunzi discussing the heart - a unique book, shared with like-minded people. Nianci's contribution cannot be ignored.

Little Western Paradise 229

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 12: Ashamed of Nakedness, Avoiding Guests Behind Curtains, Diligently Copying Books at Dawn

Young people always like young people. Ever since the encounter at Beihai, Yueying had a feeling that this man was good. Today, she was sleeping naked in someone else's quilt, and it just so happened that he arrived, which could be described as extremely coincidental. Immediately, a rush of heat rose from the soles of her feet straight to her face. Wang Beihai walked into the room and saw that the curtain was down. The door was also slightly ajar, as if Mr. Cheng wasn't sleeping in the bed. If he were sleeping in the bed, how could the door be ajar? Looking under the bed, there were no shoes either, which made it even clearer that the bed was empty. Without hesitation, he walked straight to the bedside, and just as he was about to reach out to lift the curtain, Yueying saw it very clearly and couldn't help but let out a startled cry. Wang Beihai was taken aback and took two steps back. He was stunned for a moment, then took two more steps back, thinking that it was clearly a woman's voice. How could a woman be lying in the bed of someone as proper as Mr. Cheng? This was strange. Since he wasn't in the room, it wasn't convenient for him to be here either. He should leave and close the door as if he hadn't entered, so as not to expose the matter and embarrass Mr. Cheng. Thinking this, he walked out, and just as he was leaving the room, he bumped into a tea server. He whispered with a smile, "There's a woman sleeping in Mr. Cheng's room. What's going on?" The tea server, who was a busybody, then explained how Yueying had fallen into the muddy water and was temporarily hiding here, waiting for clothes to change into. (186)

Records of Lingering Fragrance 230

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

The lives of these shoe-making artisans are also extremely monotonous; their inner selves seem to never receive any stimulation, and even slight tremors are rare. Year after year, they are solely dedicated to making phoenix shoes: waking up in the morning, working during the day, eating, and going to bed at night, doing such monotonous work every day. I myself cannot endure it, so I think that since they can enjoy it year after year, they must have an interest that outsiders cannot appreciate. I remember once asking the two leading old maids, and they both said they were very happy, the only reason being that they had a special love for this embroidery life. This shoe-making industry not only allows them to fully develop their embroidery skills, but also contains a sense of beauty in making shoe patterns, matching soles, etc., which is enough to stimulate the interest of art lovers. Their happiness probably comes from this. This is a very reasonable statement. Because no matter whom we teach to do a job, the weight of the job itself may not be a concern, the most important thing is that the job must suit the person's nature; any job that suits one's nature will surely be done with enthusiasm, and with enthusiasm, it can be done especially well and will last without getting tired. Now these two old maids are like that. As for the eight young girls under their hands? Although I have not asked them, I think the situation is roughly the same; because anyone who is not used to this work has already taken sick leave, and the rest are naturally people who are genuinely interested in it! (296)

Water Prison 231

— By Defu

"The three bitterest trades in the world are rowing boats, blacksmithing, and grinding tofu." Everyone knows this, but in addition to these three, I have discovered another bitter job, the degree of which is no less than the above three.

Every time we enter a bathhouse, we always see several back scrubbers soaked in water, their skin pale and devoid of blood. Every day, they are immersed in the water prison from 10:00 AM to 2:00 AM the next day, a total of sixteen hours. Day after day, year after year, they live like this. Even if there is a change, it is only a transfer from one water prison to another. All year round, because of the immersion in water and the steaming heat, their skin turns as white as paper, and the blood in their whole body is diluted by the water and heat. This is not all. They also have to work. Every bather, from head to toe, has to pass through their hands. After scrubbing backs, removing dirt, and bathing everyone, they sweat all over. Sweat is something everyone should have, but they sweat too much, resulting in a pale person. Living like this, no matter how strong a person is, they will weaken day by day. They themselves know that this job is harmful to the body, but they have already taken up this profession, driven by life, and they know they are entering hell, but there is no way to save it.

Rowing boats, blacksmithing, and grinding tofu are certainly bitter, but I think the back scrubbers in the bathhouse are indeed more bitter than them. Every time we bathe, we sometimes get dizzy because of the long time, but the back scrubbers have to continue working in the bathhouse for sixteen hours every day. What a painful thing this is!

I say they are sitting in a water prison, is that not an exaggeration!

Recent Poems from Jade Niche 232

— (By Shi Yun)

Inscription on a Birthday Photo

Alarmed, thirty-three springs have passed,

My age increases, but my ambition remains unfulfilled;

In the photo, my mustache and eyebrows still look fierce,

Amidst sorrow, my poems sound like the chirping of insects;

What has become of the two pills I threw away?

I'll keep my worn broom for now, cherishing it;

Realizing yesterday's wrongs, I should laugh,

From now on, I'll live a better life, starting anew.

Local Customs Sketches

Qingdao: A Japanese Hue 233

— By Nangongsheng

Qingdao was originally a desolate peninsula. After being leased to Germany during the late Qing Dynasty, the Germans gradually developed it, building fortresses and docks, and it became a good military port and summer resort in our country. In 1914, during the European War, Japan seized Qingdao while Germany was unable to look east, and regarded it as its own colony, working hard to develop it and gradually assimilate the customs of Qingdao. Although the sovereignty of most of the island was returned after negotiations at the Washington Conference, the island was already full of Japanese colors, especially in the spring when the cherry blossoms were in full bloom, fully revealing the scenery of the Japanese islands, as if it had become a Japanese semi-colony. Even the Japanese government has never forgotten that Qingdao is a place where its power can reach.

In spring, the cherry blossoms in various parts of Qingdao bloom in profusion, and can be seen everywhere. Cherry blossoms are the national flower of Japan, and when they are in full bloom, the whole country goes wild. At this time, Qingdao also holds cherry blossom festivals, and the people of the whole island play all day long, especially the Japanese residents, who are extremely happy. In the first park, shrines, and other places where cherry blossoms are planted everywhere, Japanese sentiments can be seen and heard everywhere.

Qingdao's shrines enshrine Japanese Shintoism, and many Japanese people are often seen worshiping there, but the temples of Buddhism and Taoism, which have been passed down in our country for thousands of years, have never been seen once.

Buried under the Loyal Souls Monument are the loyal souls of the Japanese soldiers who died in the battle to seize Qingdao. The style of construction is entirely Japanese in architecture and style. Similar Loyal Souls Monuments can be seen in Japan. Especially when Japanese soldiers salute at the monument, it makes people wonder if Qingdao is a Japanese colony.

The architecture on the island, apart from tall foreign houses, is mostly Japanese-style houses. In the area near Liaocheng Road, it is impossible to find a building that is not Japanese-style. The residents are all Japanese in kimonos. None of the shops sell anything but Japanese goods. Even on the most prosperous Zhongshan Road, Japanese shops are probably two-thirds of the total! The most common dishes in the small vegetable market are Japanese fish and seaweed.

There are Japanese cafes on the island, with Japanese maids arranged in the cafes. There are Japanese theaters, performing Japanese-style song and dance dramas. There are Japanese waiting places and brothels, full of Japanese prostitutes. There are Japanese police stations, Japanese restaurants, and all kinds of other shops run by Japanese people. Everything that exists in Japan is lacking in Qingdao. No wonder Japanese people can regard Qingdao as their own territory when they arrive, because the entire Qingdao area is completely Japanese in color.

Business News

Finance: Gold Speculation Initially Firm, Then Weak; Foreign Exchange Boosts Bullish Sentiment, Market Very Lively; Buyers Stand Aside, Prices Fall Back Six Yuan 234

Yesterday's gold market rose due to the continued decline in silver prices and the tightening of the foreign exchange market, and the market was quite strong. However, because sellers were active at high prices, it soon fell back. Later trading was light and lacked support, and the result was a decline. In the early morning, overseas silver markets fell across the board. Speculators said that after the market closed, transactions were made below the listed price of 0.0625 to 0.125. Forward silver markets in Montgomery were mixed, exchange rates contracted, and London spot gold did not change. Off-market pre-market trading opened and rose to over 20 yuan, but sentiment was not very firm. After opening, the central bank's listed prices were announced, both British and American currencies contracted, and the customs gold unit rose by 1.1%, and the standard gold speculation price rose to 866.7 yuan, and then rose. Although there was a setback, the banks worked hard to consolidate, and the internal market for the US dollar was very tight, and the situation was particularly strong. The banks took advantage of the high price to release sterling, and large investors sold bars and the price fell. At this time, the HSBC bank's listed prices were announced, British currency contracted by 0.125, American currency contracted by 0.3125, the foreign exchange market was still tight and there were many orders, and the white silver balance tax was announced and did not move, and had no impact. Afterwards, the Guang Bang [Guangdong merchants' guild] released some, the internal market slightly loosened, sellers were eager, and broke through the 20 yuan mark, and gradually went downstream. However, large investors bravely entered at low prices, and the bank's buying appetite was still strong, so even though Sassoon released, it was easy to pull up after the low. At noon, it was in a hovering state, and the later market was stable. The foreign exchange market was quite tight, but the gold market lacked transactions, and left the upward trend. Although there was a slight increase at one point, the buying interest was temporary, and latecomers were extremely eager, and finally settled. Indian silver fell slightly twice, and at this time there was still maintenance, and the overall situation was even more boring. Afterwards, buyers suddenly stood aside, and many short positions were closed, and rumors arose, stimulating selling. Due to the holidays, there were even fewer opponents in the market, resulting in oversupply, and a sudden drop. The market situation for the whole day was extremely calm due to the Spring Festival holiday. Now I will record the market situation for the day,

The opening price in the morning was 820.2 yuan, an increase of 1.1 yuan compared to the previous close. The central bank's customs gold listing was announced to rise by 1.1%. Fuxing, Yongheng, Yu Fu, and Yu Jin rose to 4 yuan, Hengyu, Qingfa, Yongtuo, etc., fell to 2.5 yuan. China-Belgium [bank] bought US dollars for June at 0.0625. Fuyu, Hengyu, Chunyuan, Yongchang, and Dajin rose to 4.5 yuan, Hengxing, Hengyu, and Wanxing sold bars, falling to 3 yuan. Oil Market: It's Peak Season, Asphalt May Be Difficult to Hope for Cheaply 251

The peak season for asphalt sales is just around the corner, because soap factories making soap and candle factories attacking candles are the only raw materials. The two are used in the market, especially soap making. However, the oil used in soap making only seeks cheap prices and specializes in inferior goods, while candle making does not. It is necessary to choose high-quality products and not dislike high prices, so the uses of the two are different. Tracing back to the past, due to the high price of Japanese wax, most soap factories have switched to using coconut oil, tallow, etc. as substitutes, which inevitably reduces the color of soap made with asphalt. However, the asphalt-producing areas in Sichuan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and other provinces have happened to have lean years, and the output has been greatly reduced. Therefore, although the soap is clear, there is no surplus accumulation in various producing areas. This spring, the active savings in the Han market are thin, and the sales are not very strong. Moreover, Zhejiang Province is also one of the asphalt-producing areas, and the drought last year was particularly severe. Although the year is owed, the sales field is even more owed. Most of the oil produced must be dumped to other provinces, so the market cannot be based on the Han market as usual and reduce prices on its own. In the past month, the Han market has not risen or fallen, but the Zhejiang road has fallen by about two yuan. This is because it has to reduce prices to seek distant sales in order to clear sales locally. Recently, Hanzhong and Jingmen still need 14 taels and 68 qian, Tianjin heavy 14 taels, and Macheng 14 taels and 2 qian. Because this port is close to Zhejiang Province, the sales market has been separated from the Han market for a long time. However, it will inevitably lose money if you buy it from the Han market, so those who purchase from the Han market have gradually become obsolete. Therefore, what the local dealers rely on is the Jingchi directly loaded from Yichang, which is cheaper than the Han market. However, the high and low grades of the loan products are different, so the selling price of the same Chongjing is more than two yuan higher or lower. The changes in production have reached their extreme. What can maintain the original state is only the local vehicle asphalt in Jiaxing, Western Zhejiang. It has been the same for decades and has never been high or low. Therefore, the oil sold in this port this spring seems to be more than in previous years, and it is specifically used to attack candles, because its goods are indeed welcomed by candle manufacturers, and its sales field is also increasing year by year. A month ago, it was sold for 26 yuan per load. Recently, it has fallen to 24 yuan. It is said that the active savings in the producing area are thin and there is no hope for a lower price.
